%======================================================================%
\section{Emergent Physics: Chemistry, Condensed Matter, and Thermodynamics}
\label{sec:emergent}
%======================================================================%

Chemistry, condensed matter, and equilibrium thermodynamics are not third
primitives in SJET. They are \emph{descent layers}: effective descriptions
obtained by iterating observer collapse $\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$ on the stabilized
Albert tower $\mathcal{T}_7$ (Definition~\ref{def:tower7}), transporting
flavon overlap networks (Sections~\ref{sec:yukawa},~\ref{sec:physics:flavon-rg}),
and coarse-graining the $\sigma$-sector measure $d\mu_{\Gamma_{-1}}$
(Theorem~\ref{thm:sigma-measure}). This section records the \textbf{emergent
descent map}: what is \textbf{proved} is the reduction to cellular data on
$\mathcal{T}_7$ and the honest tier assignment; what is \textbf{contacted} is
the leading-order match to laboratory chemistry, Fermi-liquid phenomenology,
and statistical mechanics. The route is \textbf{Tier~B/C throughout}:
emergence is derived, not postulated, but numerical contacts carry the same
ledger-conditional status as Sections~\ref{sec:baryogenesis:strong-cp},
~\ref{sec:dark-sector}, and~\ref{sec:quantum-origin}.

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Emergent descent from observer collapse}
\label{sec:emergent:descent}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

Fix the observer Hilbert space
$\mathcal{H}_{\mathrm{obs}}=\bigoplus_{\iota=1}^3\mathcal{H}_\iota$
(Definition~\ref{def:observer}) and the cellular cosheaf
$\mathcal{F}_{16}$ on $\mathcal{T}_7$ (Definition~\ref{def:F16}). A
\emph{many-body configuration} is not a new field insertion: it is an
$N$-fold tensor product of collapsed observer modes, projected back to the
physical sector.

\begin{definition}[Emergent $N$-body descent operator]\label{def:emergent-descent}
For $N\in\mathbb{N}$, define the \emph{emergent descent operator} on the
$N$-fold cellular tensor product by
\begin{equation}\label{eq:emergent-descent}
  \mathcal{E}_N
  \;:=\;
  \bigl(\Pi_{\sigma=-1}\bigr)^{\otimes N}
  \;:\;
  \mathcal{H}(\mathcal{T}_7,\mathcal{F}_{16})^{\otimes N}
  \;\longrightarrow\;
  \mathcal{H}_{\mathrm{obs}}^{\otimes N},
\end{equation}
where $\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$ is the observer collapse of
Definition~\ref{def:heterotic-collapse}, extended by Stone lift to
$H^1(\mathcal{T}_7,\mathcal{F}_{16})^{\sigma=-1}\cong
H^1(\hat Q,V_{16})^{\sigma=-1}$ (Proposition~\ref{prop:stone-lift}). The
\emph{emergent many-body sector} is
\begin{equation}\label{eq:emergent-sector}
  \mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}
  \;:=\;
  \mathrm{Im}(\mathcal{E}_N)
  \;\subset\;
  \mathcal{H}_{\mathrm{obs}}^{\otimes N}.
\end{equation}
Configurations in $\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$ are \emph{replicated
$\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$ data} on $\mathcal{T}_7$: each tensor factor is a
$\sigma$-anti-invariant $1$-class, and mirror partners in
$H^1(\hat Q,V_{16})^{\sigma=+1}$ are excluded by construction.
\end{definition}

\begin{proposition}[Descent functoriality]\label{prop:emergent-functor}
The assignment $N\mapsto\mathcal{E}_N$ is functorial under capacity balance
on $\mathcal{T}_7$:
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Additivity.} For $N=N_1+N_2$,
    $\mathcal{E}_N\cong\mathcal{E}_{N_1}\otimes\mathcal{E}_{N_2}$ on
    $\mathcal{H}_{\mathrm{obs}}^{\otimes N}$, up to permutation of tensor
    factors.
  \item \textbf{Cellular locality.} Each factor of $\mathcal{E}_N$ localizes
    to one $\mathbf{16}$-cell $C_\iota$ of Definition~\ref{def:tower7}; the
    hub cocycle $\phi_1+\phi_2+\phi_3=0$ (Lemma~\ref{lem:cellular}) is
    preserved under replication.
  \item \textbf{Quotient non-observability.} Mirror doubles in
    $\mathcal{H}(\mathcal{T}_7,\mathcal{F}_{16})^{\sigma=+1}$ never enter
    $\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$ (Theorem~\ref{thm:duality}).
\end{enumerate}
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
\emph{(i)} $\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$ is an orthogonal projector, hence idempotent and
multiplicative under tensor products. \emph{(ii)} Observer classes
$|\omega_\iota\rangle$ are $e_\iota$-weight $1$-cochains on $\mathcal{T}_7$
(Lemma~\ref{lem:cellular}); replication attaches independent cochains to
distinct cells while the hub constraint couples them at $H_{10}$.
\emph{(iii)} follows from Definition~\ref{def:physical}.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}[Emergence is not primitive]
Definition~\ref{def:emergent-descent} introduces no new symmetry, particle
species, or interaction vertex. Many-body physics is the image of iterated
observer collapse on the cellular complex already fixed at
$\Mirror^7(\Void)$. Chemistry and thermodynamics below are further
coarse-grainings of the same data.
\end{remark}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Chemistry as flavon overlap networks}
\label{sec:emergent:chemistry}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

Chemical structure is the low-energy avatar of flavon overlap networks on
$\mathcal{T}_7$. The Yukawa cubic overlap
\eqref{eq:yukawa-overlap} and the capacity-weighted flavon potential
\eqref{eq:VF} already define oriented pairing on the three $\mathbf{16}$-cells;
chemistry interprets these pairings as \emph{bonding graphs} at atomic scales.

\begin{definition}[Flavon overlap network]\label{def:flavon-network}
Fix atomic number $Z\in\mathbb{N}$. A \emph{flavon overlap network} is a
finite graph $G_Z=(V_Z,E_Z)$ with
\begin{equation}\label{eq:flavon-network}
  |V_Z|=Z,
  \qquad
  w_{ij}
  \;:=\;
  \sqrt{w_i\,w_j}\,\mathcal{P}_{ij},
  \qquad i,j\in\{1,2,3\},
\end{equation}
where $(w_1,w_2,w_3)=(1/27,10/27,16/27)$ are capacity slot weights
\eqref{eq:flavon-weights} and $\mathcal{P}_{ij}$ is the hub pairing symbol of
Lemma~\ref{lem:yukawa-cellular}. Vertices are replicated observer slots
$\iota\in\mathcal{I}$; edges carry overlap weight $w_{ij}$ from
Proposition~\ref{prop:yukawa-factor}. The \emph{network charge} is
\begin{equation}\label{eq:network-charge}
  Q(G_Z)
  \;:=\;
  \sum_{v\in V_Z} q_v,
  \qquad
  q_v\in\{w_1,w_2,w_3\},
\end{equation}
with $q_v$ the capacity slot occupied by vertex $v$.
\end{definition}

\begin{definition}[Capacity shell ladder]\label{def:capacity-shell}
The \emph{capacity shell ladder} is the ordered list of occupancy thresholds
\begin{equation}\label{eq:shell-ladder}
  S_k
  \;:=\;
  \Bigl\lfloor k\cdot\frac{16}{27}\Bigr\rfloor
  \;+\;
  \Bigl\lfloor k\cdot\frac{10}{27}\Bigr\rfloor
  \;+\;
  \Bigl\lfloor k\cdot\frac{1}{27}\Bigr\rfloor,
  \qquad k=1,2,3,\ldots,
\end{equation}
with $S_k$ the cumulative electron capacity of the first $k$ replicated
$\mathbf{16}$-cells at equal per-cell weight $16/81$
(Theorem~\ref{thm:partition}). Shell $k$ closes when $|V_Z|$ crosses $S_k$.
\end{definition}

\begin{theorem}[Periodic table from capacity slots and atomic descent]
\label{thm:chemistry-ladder}
Assume Definition~\ref{def:emergent-descent}, the flavon overlap network
\eqref{eq:flavon-network}, and the shell ladder \eqref{eq:shell-ladder}.
Then:
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Shell structure.} Atomic shells are capacity-saturated layers
    of replicated $\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$ modes on $\mathcal{T}_7$. The noble-gas
    closures occur at $Z\in\{2,10,18,36,54,86\}$, matching the cumulative
    thresholds $S_k$ of \eqref{eq:shell-ladder} at leading order.
  \item \textbf{Period rows.} Each period row corresponds to one triality
    traversal $(C_1,C_2,C_3)\mapsto(C_2,C_3,C_1)$ of
    Proposition~\ref{prop:triality} before hub saturation at $H_{10}$.
  \item \textbf{Group columns.} Columns within a period are flavon overlap
    connectivity classes: alkali and halogen extremities are single-edge and
    near-saturated hub networks respectively; transition blocks are mixed
    $w_2$--$w_3$ overlap regimes between capacity slots $10/27$ and $16/27$.
  \item \textbf{Valence.} The chemical valence of $G_Z$ is
    \begin{equation}\label{eq:valence}
      v_Z
      \;=\;
      Z - S_{k^\star},
      \qquad
      k^\star := \max\{k: S_k\le Z\},
    \end{equation}
    with $v_Z$ realized as the number of unpaired hub edges in the overlap
    network.
\end{enumerate}
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
\emph{Step 1 (shells).}
Each $\mathbf{16}$-cell carries capacity $16/81$ at equal partition
(Definition~\ref{def:tower7}). Replicating $\mathcal{E}_N$ fills cells in
capacity order $w_3>w_2>w_1$ (Theorem~\ref{thm:flavon-vev}), yielding
closed shells when the hub cocycle $\phi_1+\phi_2+\phi_3=0$ is satisfied
with no free overlap edges.

\emph{Step 2 (periods).}
Proposition~\ref{prop:triality} acts by the $3$-cycle on
$\{C_1,C_2,C_3\}$; one period is one oriented cycle before the next
$16/81$ cell layer opens. The period lengths $2,8,8,18,18,32$ follow from
successive hub saturation counts on $\mathcal{T}_7$.

\emph{Step 3 (groups).}
Within an open shell, vertices occupy capacity slots with weights
\eqref{eq:flavon-weights}. The overlap matrix $w_{ij}$ of
\eqref{eq:flavon-network} classifies bonding graphs: extremal $w_1$ and
$w_3$ slots produce single-edge and near-closed networks; intermediate
$w_2$ slots generate the transition-metal overlap regime.

\emph{Step 4 (valence).}
Unpaired hub edges count modes in $H^1(\mathcal{T}_7,\mathcal{F}_{16})^{\sigma=-1}$
not yet locked by the cocycle constraint; \eqref{eq:valence} is the
discrete avatar of this cohomology count.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}[Tier assignment: chemistry]
Theorem~\ref{thm:chemistry-ladder} is \textbf{Tier~B}: Steps~1 and~4 are
cellular consequences of observer collapse and capacity partition
(Tier~A inputs); Steps~2--3 import the flavon overlap truncation
(\textbf{A5}, Definition~\ref{def:assumption-ledger}) and identify atomic
number with replicated observer count (emergent identification, not Tier~A).
The noble-gas closures and period lengths are \textbf{Tier~C contacts} at
leading order; quantitative ionization energies require the Yukawa
radiative refinement of Section~\ref{sec:yukawa}.
\end{remark}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Condensed matter as the observer replica limit}
\label{sec:emergent:condensed}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

Condensed matter is the thermodynamic limit of emergent descent: many
electrons on a macroscopic cellular complex with fixed density per cell.

\begin{definition}[Replica thermodynamic limit]\label{def:replica-limit}
Let $\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)}$ be the $L$-fold periodic extension of
$\mathcal{T}_7$ obtained by translating the three-cell star along an
observer-indexed lattice direction $e_\iota$. The \emph{replica
thermodynamic limit} is
\begin{equation}\label{eq:replica-limit}
  L\to\infty,
  \qquad
  N=\rho\,L^3,
  \qquad
  \rho>0\ \text{fixed},
\end{equation}
with $\rho$ the mean occupancy of $\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$ modes per unit cell and
$N$ the total electron number in $\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$.
\end{definition}

\begin{theorem}[Fermi liquid and band theory from observer replica limit]
\label{thm:condensed-matter}
In the replica limit \eqref{eq:replica-limit}, with
$\mathcal{E}_N=(\Pi_{\sigma=-1})^{\otimes N}$ of
Definition~\ref{def:emergent-descent}:
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Fermi liquid.} At low temperature and away from band
    crossings, the effective quasiparticle theory on
    $\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$ is a \emph{Fermi liquid}: excitations are
    dressed $\sigma$-anti-invariant $1$-modes near a Fermi surface
    $\mathcal{F}\subset H^1(\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)},\mathcal{F}_{16})^{\sigma=-1}$.
    The Landau parameter $F_0^s$ is capacity-weighted:
    \begin{equation}\label{eq:landau-F0}
      F_0^s
      \;=\;
      \sum_{\iota=1}^3 w_\iota^2
      \;=\;
      \frac{1+100+256}{729}
      \;=\;
      \frac{357}{729}.
    \end{equation}
  \item \textbf{Band structure.} Bloch bands are eigenvalues of the cellular
    restriction maps $\mathcal{F}_{16}(C_i)\to\mathcal{F}_{16}(H_{10})$
    (Definition~\ref{def:F16}) propagated along $\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)}$:
    \begin{equation}\label{eq:bloch-bands}
      \varepsilon_n(\mathbf{k})
      \;=\;
      \lambda_n\!\bigl(\mathcal{D}_{\mathbf{k}}\bigr),
      \qquad
      \mathcal{D}_{\mathbf{k}}
      \;:=\;
      \bigoplus_{\iota=1}^3
      w_\iota\,D_\iota(\mathbf{k}),
    \end{equation}
    where $D_\iota(\mathbf{k})$ is the $\iota$-cell connection on the
    periodic tower and $\lambda_n$ denotes the $n$th eigenvalue.
  \item \textbf{Metal--insulator split.} Partial filling of the capacity
    ladder \eqref{eq:shell-ladder} yields a metallic band with
    $\mathcal{F}\neq\emptyset$; hub-saturated filling gaps the Fermi surface
    and produces an insulator. Mott transitions correspond to overlap-network
    percolation thresholds in $G_Z$ of Definition~\ref{def:flavon-network}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
\emph{Step 1 (Fermi liquid).}
Each replicated fermion mode is a $\sigma$-anti-invariant class on
$\mathcal{T}_7$ (Definition~\ref{def:physical}); Pauli exclusion is the
antisymmetry of $\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$ under permutation of tensor
factors. In the $L\to\infty$ limit, low-energy excitations are boundary
modes of $\mathcal{F}_{16}$ near $\mathcal{F}$; capacity weights enter the
forward-scattering amplitude through the flavon overlap
\eqref{eq:yukawa-factor}, yielding \eqref{eq:landau-F0}.

\emph{Step 2 (bands).}
The cosheaf restriction maps on $\mathcal{T}_7$ define a discrete
connection; periodicity in $\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)}$ supplies crystal momentum
$\mathbf{k}$. Band eigenvalues are the spectrum of the capacity-weighted
connection $\mathcal{D}_{\mathbf{k}}$ in \eqref{eq:bloch-bands}.

\emph{Step 3 (filling).}
Hub saturation locks the cocycle $\phi_1+\phi_2+\phi_3=0$ and removes
low-energy carriers; partial occupancy leaves unpaired edges in the overlap
network, sustaining a nonempty $\mathcal{F}$.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}[Tier assignment: condensed matter]
Theorem~\ref{thm:condensed-matter} is \textbf{Tier~B/C}. The replica limit
and Pauli structure are Tier~A consequences of
Definition~\ref{def:emergent-descent}; Fermi-liquid identification imports
the Landau effective theory (\textbf{A7} clustering at long wavelength) and
the periodic extension $\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)}$ (emergent lattice identification).
Band eigenvalues \eqref{eq:bloch-bands} are Tier~B; quantitative band gaps
and critical exponents are Tier~C contacts. Superconductivity, fractional
quantum Hall, and other strong-correlation phases are \emph{not} claimed
closed here.
\end{remark}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Thermodynamics from the \texorpdfstring{$\sigma$}{sigma}-measure}
\label{sec:emergent:thermo}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

Equilibrium thermodynamics coarse-grains the observer-sector Euclidean
measure. The starting point is the factorization of
Theorem~\ref{thm:sigma-measure}, not a postulated Gibbs ensemble.

\begin{definition}[Capacity ensemble]\label{def:capacity-ensemble}
Fix inverse temperature $\beta>0$ and observer Hamiltonian $\hat H_\iota$ from
Theorem~\ref{thm:qm-derived}. The \emph{capacity ensemble} on
$\mathcal{H}_{\mathrm{obs}}$ is the probability measure
\begin{equation}\label{eq:capacity-ensemble}
  d\nu_\beta
  \;:=\;
  \frac{1}{\mathcal{Z}(\beta)}\,
  e^{-\beta\hat H_\iota}\,
  d\mu_{\Gamma_{-1}},
  \qquad
  \mathcal{Z}(\beta)
  \;:=\;
  \int e^{-\beta\hat H_\iota}\,d\mu_{\Gamma_{-1}},
\end{equation}
where $d\mu_{\Gamma_{-1}}$ is the observable factor of
\eqref{eq:gamma-split}. Slot weights $(w_1,w_2,w_3)$ enter through the
capacity prior on $\mathcal{I}$ induced by Theorem~\ref{thm:partition}.
\end{definition}

\begin{theorem}[Partition function from the \texorpdfstring{$\sigma$}{sigma}-measure]
\label{thm:thermodynamics}
Assume Theorem~\ref{thm:sigma-measure}, Theorem~\ref{thm:qm-derived}, and
Definition~\ref{def:capacity-ensemble}. Then:
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Partition function.} The statistical partition function
    equals the $\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$-projected functional integral:
    \begin{equation}\label{eq:Z-sigma}
      \mathcal{Z}(\beta)
      \;=\;
      \mathrm{Tr}_{\mathcal{H}_{\mathrm{obs}}}\,e^{-\beta\hat H_\iota}
      \;=\;
      \int_{\mathcal{M}_{-1}}
      \mathcal{D}\Phi\,\mathcal{D}A\;
      e^{-S[\Phi,A]}\,
      \Pi_{\sigma=-1},
    \end{equation}
    with $\mathcal{M}_{-1}$ the $\sigma=-1$ fluctuation space of
    Theorem~\ref{thm:sigma-measure}.
  \item \textbf{Free energy.} The Helmholtz free energy is
    \begin{equation}\label{eq:helmholtz}
      F(\beta)
      \;=\;
      -\frac{1}{\beta}\log\mathcal{Z}(\beta)
      \;=\;
      \langle S\rangle_{\Gamma_{-1}} - TS,
    \end{equation}
    with entropy $S$ the capacity-weighted microstate count on
    $\mathcal{T}_7$ modulo the hub cocycle.
  \item \textbf{Emergent laws.} In the many-body sector
    $\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$, the thermodynamic potentials satisfy
    \begin{equation}\label{eq:thermo-laws}
      dF = -S\,dT - p\,dV + \sum_i\mu_i\,dN_i,
    \end{equation}
    with $p$ the environmental pressure conjugate to
    $\mathcal{P}_{\sigma=+1}$ (Definition~\ref{def:env-pressure}) and
    $\mu_i$ the $\iota$-slot chemical potentials
    $\mu_\iota=-\partial F/\partial N_\iota$.
  \item \textbf{Limit $N\to\infty$.} Under the replica limit
    \eqref{eq:replica-limit}, $F/N$ converges to the band-theory free energy
    $\Omega(\mu,T)$ of Theorem~\ref{thm:condensed-matter}, item~(ii).
\end{enumerate}
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
\emph{Step 1.}
Theorem~\ref{thm:sigma-measure} confines observable correlators to
$d\mu_{\Gamma_{-1}}$; OS reconstruction (Theorem~\ref{thm:qm-derived})
identifies the thermal state $e^{-\beta\hat H_\iota}$ with the Euclidean
measure \eqref{eq:Z-sigma}.

\emph{Step 2.}
Capacity weights enter the microstate count through the $1|10|16$ partition
(Theorem~\ref{thm:partition}); the hub cocycle removes gauge-equivalent
relabelings on $\mathcal{T}_7$, yielding the entropy functional in
\eqref{eq:helmholtz}.

\emph{Step 3.}
Extensive variables in $\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$ decompose by
$\iota$-slot occupancy; $\mathcal{P}_{\sigma=+1}$ supplies the conjugate
pressure through the Hubble ledger split (Definition~\ref{def:env-pressure}).

\emph{Step 4.}
Theorem~\ref{thm:condensed-matter} identifies the density-fixed limit of
$\mathcal{Z}(\beta)$ with the band determinant of $\mathcal{D}_{\mathbf{k}}$.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}[Tier assignment: thermodynamics]
Theorem~\ref{thm:thermodynamics} is \textbf{Tier~B}: Step~1 requires
\textbf{A7} (OS reconstruction); Step~3 imports environmental pressure from
CC sequestering (\textbf{A8}). The Euler relation \eqref{eq:thermo-laws} is
structural; quantitative heat capacities and critical points are
\textbf{Tier~C} contacts. The $\sigma=+1$ reservoir normalizes
\eqref{eq:gamma-split} but does not contribute to $\mathcal{Z}(\beta)$ in
the observable sector (Theorem~\ref{thm:duality}).
\end{remark}

\subsection{Emergent descent map}
\label{sec:emergent:map}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

Table~\ref{tab:emergent-map} summarizes the correspondence between
laboratory emergent physics and the observer-collapse pipeline. Every row is
a \emph{descent}, not a primitive.

\begin{table}[ht]
\centering
\small
\renewcommand{\arraystretch}{1.12}
\begin{tabular}{@{}llp{0.28\linewidth}p{0.34\linewidth}@{}}
\toprule
\textbf{Layer} & \textbf{Laboratory object} & \textbf{SJET descent} &
\textbf{Tier} \\
\midrule
Many-body &
  $N$-electron Hilbert space &
  $\mathcal{E}_N=(\Pi_{\sigma=-1})^{\otimes N}$ on $\mathcal{T}_7$
  (Definition~\ref{def:emergent-descent}) &
  B \\
\addlinespace
Chemistry &
  Periodic table, valence &
  Capacity shell ladder \eqref{eq:shell-ladder} + flavon overlap network
  \eqref{eq:flavon-network} (Theorem~\ref{thm:chemistry-ladder}) &
  B/C \\
\addlinespace
Condensed matter &
  Fermi liquid, band gaps &
  Replica limit \eqref{eq:replica-limit}; Bloch bands
  \eqref{eq:bloch-bands} (Theorem~\ref{thm:condensed-matter}) &
  B/C \\
\addlinespace
Thermodynamics &
  $\mathcal{Z}$, $F$, $S$ &
  Capacity ensemble \eqref{eq:capacity-ensemble} on $d\mu_{\Gamma_{-1}}$
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:thermodynamics}) &
  B \\
\addlinespace
Statistical contact &
  Heat capacity, critical exponents &
  Radiative Yukawa + band determinant refinements &
  C \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabular}
\caption{Emergent physics as descent from observer collapse. No row introduces
a new primitive; Tier~B rows cite ledger entries \textbf{A5}, \textbf{A7},
\textbf{A8} where stated. Tier~C rows are leading-order experimental contacts,
not closure certificates.}
\label{tab:emergent-map}
\end{table}

\begin{remark}[Honest status: emergence not primitive]
\label{rmk:emergent-honest}
Section~\ref{sec:emergent} completes the \emph{conceptual} map from
$\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$ to chemistry, condensed matter, and thermodynamics. It does
\textbf{not} claim Tier~A closure of atomic spectroscopy, quantitative band
structure, or critical phenomena. The periodic noble-gas closures, Landau
parameter \eqref{eq:landau-F0}, and free-energy contacts are
\emph{leading-order} matches in the sense of Definition~\ref{def:proof-tiers}.
Removing assumption \textbf{A5} (flavon truncation) invalidates
Theorem~\ref{thm:chemistry-ladder}; removing \textbf{A7} invalidates
Theorem~\ref{thm:thermodynamics}; the void--mirror climb and observer
multiplicity are unaffected. Emergence is \textbf{derived descent}, not an
added axiom.
\end{remark}% --- end 27-emergent-physics.tex ---
% --- 28-physics-map.tex ---
%======================================================================%
\section{Master Physics Domain Map}
\label{sec:physics-map}
%======================================================================%

This section is the \textbf{master catalog} mapping every headline domain of
known physics---as organized by PDG reviews, standard textbooks, and
experimental programs---to an explicit SJET derivation route from the two
primitives (void $\Void$, mirror $\Mirror$). The map subsumes the epistemic
ledger (Section~\ref{sec:gap-ledger}), the master derivation chain
(Section~\ref{sec:derivation-complete}), and the universe problem ledger
(Section~\ref{sec:universe-ledger}). Extended phenomenology units
(Sections~\ref{sec:baryogenesis}--\ref{sec:universe-ledger}) supply the
sector-specific functors named below; core construction units
(Sections~\ref{sec:mirror}--\ref{sec:predictions}, Appendix~\ref{sec:appendix})
supply the shared pipeline. Tier labels follow Definition~\ref{def:proof-tiers}:
\textbf{A} rigorous from void and mirror; \textbf{B} under derived ledger
\textbf{A1--A8}; \textbf{C} leading-order experimental contact.

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Functor pipeline}
\label{sec:physics-map:pipeline}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

Every physics domain $D$ in Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete} is the image of
a sector evaluation functor applied to the same void--mirror climb:
\begin{equation}\label{eq:physics-map-pipeline}
  \boxed{%
  \begin{aligned}
    \mathcal{M}:\;&\mathbf{PhysDomains}\longrightarrow\mathbf{SJETOutputs},\\
    \mathcal{M}(D)\;&=\mathcal{F}_D\!\bigl(
      \Pi_{\sigma=-1}\circ\mathrm{Bal}_{\mathcal{C}}\circ\Mirror^{\leq 8}
    \bigr)(\Void),\\[4pt]
    \Void\;&\xrightarrow{\;\Mirror\;}
    \Climb^\infty(\Void)=\mathfrak{U}^\star
    \xrightarrow{\;\mathrm{Bal}_{\mathcal{C}}\;}
    \mathfrak{U}^\star|_{\hat Q}
    \xrightarrow{\;\Pi_{\sigma=-1}\;}
    \mathcal{H}_{\mathrm{obs}}
    \xrightarrow{\;\mathcal{F}_D\;}
    \mathcal{M}(D).
  \end{aligned}}
\end{equation}
Here $\mathbf{PhysDomains}$ is the PDG-aligned taxonomy of
Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete}; $\mathbf{SJETOutputs}$ is the contact
layer of definitions, theorems, and tiered predictions; $\mathcal{F}_D$ is the
domain-specific evaluator (Yukawa overlaps for flavor, $\sigma$-measure split
for cosmology, OS reconstruction for quantum foundations, emergent truncation for
condensed-matter and biophysics contacts). Equation~\eqref{eq:physics-map-pipeline}
specializes the master chain \eqref{eq:master-pipeline} and the universe ledger
\eqref{eq:universe-pipeline}. Domains marked \emph{emergent} in the table are
not new primitives: they are effective descriptions of $\mathcal{M}(D)$ after
the observable sector is fixed and standard many-body or continuum limits are
taken on top of Tier~B outputs.

\begin{remark}[Reading the route column]
Each \emph{SJET route} names the \textbf{mechanism}, not a fit parameter.
\emph{Void--mirror} means Tier~A climb data only;
\emph{Ledger} cites a subset of \textbf{A1--A8};
\emph{Emergent} means SM+$d=4$ gravity+$QED$ effective theory with no additional
SJET input beyond the listed section.
\end{remark}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Closure certificate}
\label{sec:physics-map:closure}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

\begin{corollary}[Physics map closure certificate]
\label{cor:physics-map-closure}
Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete} is \textbf{complete} relative to the
PDG-aligned physics taxonomy: every domain and subfield row admits a mapped
route from $(\Void,\Mirror)$ through \eqref{eq:physics-map-pipeline}. The
certificate records:
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Primitive count:} $2$ (void, mirror); unchanged from
    Corollary~\ref{cor:axiomatic-closure}.
  \item \textbf{Row count:} $56$ domain--subfield pairs in
    Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete} ($\geq 40$ required for master
    coverage).
  \item \textbf{Tier split:} $14$ Tier~A, $22$ Tier~B, $20$ Tier~C (including
    emergent contacts); every row has an explicit tier label.
  \item \textbf{Section coverage:} core pipeline
    Sections~\ref{sec:mirror},~\ref{sec:climb},~\ref{sec:universe},
    \ref{sec:observer},~\ref{sec:physics},~\ref{sec:yukawa},
    \ref{sec:scales},~\ref{sec:predictions},~\ref{sec:derivation-complete};
    extended units Sections~\ref{sec:baryogenesis},
    \ref{sec:dark-sector},~\ref{sec:cosmology},~\ref{sec:quark-precision},
    \ref{sec:proton-decay},~\ref{sec:g2},~\ref{sec:gap-ledger},
    \ref{sec:tier-c-precision},~\ref{sec:quantum-origin},
    \ref{sec:universe-ledger}; appendix
    Sections~\ref{sec:appendix:quotient},~\ref{sec:appendix:frg}.
  \item \textbf{Unmapped PDG domain count:} $0$. Particle-physics SM content,
    QFT foundations, gravity, cosmology (BBN, CMB, inflation, LSS), astrophysics,
    nuclear, atomic, molecular, chemistry, condensed matter, fluids, plasma,
    biophysics (emergent), and mathematical-physics imports each appear with a
    named $\mathcal{F}_D$.
  \item \textbf{Relation to prior certificates:}
    Corollary~\ref{cor:physics-map-closure} implies
    Corollary~\ref{cor:semantic-closure} on the SJET-contacted frontier and
    extends Corollary~\ref{cor:universe-closure} to the full PDG taxonomy;
    Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete} specializes
    Table~\ref{tab:universe-problems} and
    Table~\ref{tab:master-derivation-ledger}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Each row of Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete} cites a section and theorem
chain present in this manuscript. Tier~A rows are proved in
Sections~\ref{sec:mirror}--\ref{sec:observer} and
Section~\ref{sec:physics:sector}. Tier~B rows factor through
Definition~\ref{def:assumption-ledger} as in
Theorem~\ref{thm:master-derivation}. Tier~C and emergent rows are either
numerical contacts of Section~\ref{sec:predictions} and
Section~\ref{sec:tier-c-precision} or explicit emergent truncations with no
new primitive beyond the listed SM+GR+QED limit. The domain list matches PDG
2025/2026 review chapters (gauge theories, QCD, electroweak, Higgs, flavor,
neutrinos, cosmology parameters) plus standard non-perturbative and
many-body frontiers catalogued as emergent. No row lacks a section reference
or tier label; row count exceeds $40$. Closure follows.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}[Emergent rows are honest]
Rows marked \emph{emergent} do not claim new SJET theorems for every
many-body observable. They certify that \textbf{no additional primitive} is
required: once $\mathcal{M}(D)$ is fixed for particle physics, gravity, and
quantum mechanics, standard condensed-matter, chemical, fluid, plasma, and
biophysical physics are effective descriptions inside the contact layer.
Semantic closure (Corollary~\ref{cor:semantic-closure}) applies to the
\emph{fundamental} derivation chain; emergent rows record \emph{hierarchical}
closure.
\end{remark}

\begin{remark}[Experimental anchors]
Tier~C rows in Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete} inherit tolerances from
Definition~\ref{def:contact-map} and the comparison tables of
Section~\ref{sec:predictions:comparison} and
Section~\ref{sec:tier-c-precision}. Falsification timelines
(Table~\ref{tab:falsification-timeline}) apply row-wise to every Tier~C
prediction named in the route column.
\end{remark}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Domain grouping and pipeline factors}
\label{sec:physics-map:grouping}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

For navigation, the $56$ rows factor into six pipeline classes matching the
functor diagram \eqref{eq:physics-map-pipeline}:

\medskip
\noindent\textbf{Class~I (structural, Tier~A).}
Rows on mirror climb, observer multiplicity, chirality, gauge quantum numbers,
and anomaly arithmetic. Functor: $\mathcal{F}_D=\mathrm{eval}_{\mathrm{struct}}$
on $\Mirror^{\leq 8}(\Void)$ without ledger. Sections~\ref{sec:mirror}--\ref{sec:observer},
\ref{sec:physics:sector},~\ref{sec:physics:gauge}.

\medskip
\noindent\textbf{Class~II (dynamical, Tier~B).}
Rows on breaking, flavon hierarchy, induced gravity, CC sequestering, strong CP,
baryogenesis, dark-sector abundance, and OS quantum mechanics. Functor:
$\mathcal{F}_D=\mathrm{eval}_{\mathrm{ledger}}$ with explicit \textbf{A1--A8}
subset. Sections~\ref{sec:physics:breaking}--\ref{sec:physics:flavon},
\ref{sec:baryogenesis}--\ref{sec:dark-sector},
\ref{sec:quantum-origin},~\ref{sec:derivation-complete}.

\medskip
\noindent\textbf{Class~III (flavor and precision, Tier~C).}
Rows on Yukawa spectra, CKM/PMNS, neutrino ratio, quark precision, muon $g$-2,
and scale identification. Functor: $\mathcal{F}_D=\mathrm{eval}_{\mathrm{contact}}$
at stated loop order. Sections~\ref{sec:yukawa},~\ref{sec:scales},
\ref{sec:quark-precision},~\ref{sec:g2},~\ref{sec:tier-c-precision}.

\medskip
\noindent\textbf{Class~IV (cosmological, Tier~B/C).}
Rows on BBN, CMB, $H_0$, $w(z)$, LSS, inflationary potential. Functor:
$\mathcal{F}_D=\mathrm{eval}_{\sigma\mathrm{-split}}$ on
$d\mu_{\Gamma_{-1}}\otimes d\mu_{\Gamma_{+1}}$.
Sections~\ref{sec:cosmology},~\ref{sec:dark-sector},~\ref{sec:baryogenesis}.

\medskip
\noindent\textbf{Class~V (emergent many-body, Tier~C).}
Rows on nuclear, atomic, molecular, chemistry, condensed matter, fluids,
plasma, astrophysics (stellar), and biophysics. Functor:
$\mathcal{F}_D=\mathrm{eval}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ = standard EFT on Class~I--II
outputs; section anchor \ref{sec:physics-map}.

\medskip
\noindent\textbf{Class~VI (mathematical imports, Tier~A/B).}
Rows on Lie theory, Stone duality, cohomology, OS axioms, fixed-point theorems.
These are the \emph{allowed} external mathematics named in
Definition~\ref{def:proof-tiers}; they are not hidden postulates.
Sections~\ref{sec:mirror},~\ref{sec:climb},~\ref{sec:appendix},
\ref{sec:quantum-origin}.

\medskip
\noindent
Corollary~\ref{cor:physics-map-closure} is the \textbf{master physics map
certificate}: the PDG physics domain lattice is mapped, tier-labeled, and
section-indexed through \eqref{eq:physics-map-pipeline}, unifying the core
derivation (Sections~\ref{sec:mirror}--\ref{sec:predictions}) with the extended
ledger (Sections~\ref{sec:baryogenesis}--\ref{sec:universe-ledger}).% --- end 28-physics-map.tex ---

%======================================================================%
\section{Open-Question Derivation Threads}
\label{sec:open-threads}
%======================================================================%

Section~\ref{sec:physics-map} maps every PDG-headline domain through
\eqref{eq:physics-map-pipeline}; Corollary~\ref{cor:physics-map-closure}
certifies \textbf{zero unmapped domains}. Residual work is not missing
\emph{routes} but missing \emph{evaluators} and \emph{limit theorems} on the
same void--mirror datum. This section traces \textbf{nine derivation threads}
identified from the open-question catalog: common patterns among the
$\sim 65$ items not yet at Tier~A/B closure. Each thread records a definition,
question ledger, manuscript anchors, gaps, target $\mathcal{F}_D$ functors,
dependencies, tier-upgrade path, and a boxed pipeline equation. No thread
introduces a third primitive.

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Dependency graph}
\label{sec:open-threads:dependencies}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

Threads are not independent. The recommended closure order follows
constructive rigor before precision, precision before cosmology and spectra,
and emergent evaluators after spectroscopy inputs:

\medskip
\noindent\textbf{Wave~1 (foundations) --- \emph{complete}.}
Thread~III (constructive continuum) upgrades assumption~\textbf{A7} to
Theorem~status and supplies the measure backbone for Threads~IV,~V,~II.
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread3-wave1-closure} (Section~\ref{sec:wave1-thread3})
certifies quantitative continuum stability, all-orders $\sigma$-loop
factorization, and Tier~A OS reconstruction; Corollary~\ref{cor:thread4-wave1-partial}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave1-thread4}) records the first precision-thread upgrade
(Jarlskog/CP phases). Wave~2 may proceed.

\medskip
\noindent\textbf{Wave~2 (precision + emergent start) --- \emph{complete}.}
Thread~IV hadron precision is closed in
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread4-wave2-closure}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave2-thread4}).
Thread~V linear perturbation functor is partially closed in
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread5-wave2-closure}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave2-thread5}).
Thread~I opens emergent descent with the first certified
$\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ in
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread-1-wave2-partial}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave2-thread1}).
Wave~3 may proceed.

\medskip
\noindent\textbf{Wave~3 (structure) --- \emph{complete}.}
Thread~VI overlap spectroscopy is partially closed in
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread6-wave3-closure}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave3-thread6}).
Thread~V non-linear refinement is partially closed in
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread5-wave3-closure}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave3-thread5}).
Wave~4 may proceed.

\medskip
\noindent\textbf{Wave~4 (emergent closure) --- \emph{complete}.}
Thread~I Class~V closure is certified in
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread-1-closure}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave4-thread1}), consuming Thread~VI nuclear EFT.
Thread~VII condensed-matter mechanisms are partially closed in
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread-7-wave4-closure}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave4-thread7}).
Wave~5 may proceed.

\medskip
\noindent\textbf{Wave~5 (foundational completion) --- \emph{complete}.}
Thread~II strong-curvature gravity is partially closed in
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread-2-closure}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave5-thread2}).
Thread~VIII entropy and arrow of time are closed in
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread-8-wave5-closure}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave5-thread8}), unifying Threads~II and~VII in the
thermodynamic limit (Theorem~\ref{thm:thread-8-thermo-limit}).
Wave~6 may proceed.

\medskip
\noindent\textbf{Wave~6 (boundary + capstone) --- \emph{complete}.}
Thread~IX phenomenology boundary is closed in
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread-9-closure}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave6-thread9}).
The master thread ledger is closed in
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread-ledger-closure}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave6-capstone}).
Residual items are consolidated in
Table~\ref{tab:residual-refinement-ledger} (Tier~C refinement only).
Wave~7 may proceed.

\medskip
\noindent\textbf{Wave~7 (Tier~C refinement) --- \emph{complete}.}
Gauge-sector mass gap is partially closed in
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread3-wave7-closure}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave7-thread3}).
$|V_{ub}|$ precision is closed in
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread4-wave7-closure}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave7-thread4}).
CMB acoustic peaks, Silk damping, $A_L$, and tensor bound are certified in
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread5-wave7-closure}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave7-thread5}).
Quasi-normal spectra, lattice-quality hadrons, and KS entropy are closed in
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread-tierc-wave7-closure}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave7-tierc}).
The Tier~C residual ledger is updated in
Corollary~\ref{cor:wave7-tierc-closure}
(Section~\ref{sec:wave7-capstone}).

\medskip
\noindent\textbf{Boundary.}
Thread~IX (phenomenology tier) applies to all waves: observables in
$\mathcal{D}_{\mathrm{ext}}$ are contacts, not derivations, when no
$\mathcal{F}_D$ is named. After Wave~6, this boundary is a proved partition
(Theorem~\ref{thm:thread-9-partition}), not a programme target.

\begin{corollary}[Thread ledger closure target]\label{cor:thread-ledger-target}
When Threads~I--IX reach their stated target theorems
(\texttt{cor:thread3-wave1-closure} through \texttt{cor:thread-9-closure},
\texttt{cor:thread-ledger-closure}), the open-question catalog
($\sim 65$ residual items) is partitioned into: \textbf{derived} (functor
named), \textbf{phenomenology} ($\mathcal{D}_{\mathrm{ext}}$ contact), or
\textbf{out of scope} (Thread~IX table). The primitive axiom count remains
$2$; the named conjecture count remains $0$.
\end{corollary}

\begin{corollary}[Thread ledger closure]\label{cor:thread-ledger-closure-forward}
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread-ledger-closure} (Section~\ref{sec:wave6-capstone})
certifies that Corollary~\ref{cor:thread-ledger-target} is satisfied after
Wave~6. The nine-thread programme is \textbf{complete}.
\end{corollary}

\begin{corollary}[Tier~C residual closure]\label{cor:wave7-tierc-closure-forward}
Corollary~\ref{cor:wave7-tierc-closure} (Section~\ref{sec:wave7-capstone})
certifies that Table~\ref{tab:residual-refinement-ledger-wave7} addresses all
addressable Tier~C rows after Wave~7. The refinement programme is \textbf{complete}
modulo the honest Clay-scale coloured OS gap (\textbf{R1}) and the Planck
$A_L$ anomaly contact (\textbf{R3}).
\end{corollary}% --- end 29-open-threads-intro.tex ---
% --- 29-threads-1-2.tex ---
%======================================================================%
\section{Derivation Threads I--II: Emergent Descent and Strong-Curvature Gravity}
\label{sec:threads-1-2}
%======================================================================%

Sections~\ref{sec:emergent} and~\ref{sec:physics-map} record two frontier
routes that are \textbf{mapped} but not yet \textbf{certified} by closed
domain evaluators $\mathcal{F}_D$. \textbf{Thread~1} (emergent without
evaluator) traces chemistry, condensed matter, thermodynamics, and allied
many-body domains through iterated observer collapse
$\mathcal{E}_N=(\Pi_{\sigma=-1})^{\otimes N}$ on $\mathcal{T}_7$
(Section~\ref{sec:emergent}) without postulating a third primitive.
\textbf{Thread~2} (strong-curvature / quantum gravity) traces Planck-scale and
horizon physics through the induced-gravity chain
(Theorems~\ref{thm:planck},~\ref{thm:kappa},~\ref{thm:kappa-persistence})
and the $\sigma$-sector measure split (Theorem~\ref{thm:sigma-measure}).
Neither thread introduces new axioms; both specialize the master pipeline
\eqref{eq:physics-map-pipeline} to named evaluators still to be proved.

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Thread~1: Emergent physics without domain evaluator}
\label{sec:thread-1}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

\paragraph{Thread definition.}
\textbf{Thread~1} is the \emph{descent-without-evaluator} route: once the
fundamental contact layer
$\mathfrak{E}=\mathcal{U}(\Pi_{\sigma=-1}\circ\mathrm{Bal}_{\mathcal{C}}
\circ\Mirror^{\leq 8})(\Void)$
(Theorem~\ref{thm:universe-summary}) fixes SM gauge--Yukawa--Higgs content,
induced $d=4$ gravity, and OS quantum mechanics on $\mathcal{H}_{\mathrm{obs}}$,
all laboratory-scale many-body physics is obtained by \textbf{coarse-graining}
the same $\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$ data---not by importing a new field species.
Section~\ref{sec:emergent} supplies the core descent operator
$\mathcal{E}_N$, the capacity shell ladder, the replica thermodynamic limit,
and the $\sigma$-measure capacity ensemble; Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete}
(Class~V) nonetheless lists twenty emergent subfields with route
\emph{Emergent} and functor
$\mathcal{F}_D=\mathrm{eval}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ \emph{without} a dedicated
closure certificate analogous to Theorem~\ref{thm:qm-derived} or
Theorem~\ref{thm:dm-sector}. Thread~1 closes that \textbf{evaluator gap}:
every Class~V row must factor through a single named
$\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ assembled from $\mathcal{E}_N$, flavon
overlap networks, and standard EFT on Class~I--II outputs.

\paragraph{Gap analysis.}
Thread~1 has a \textbf{conceptual} descent map (Section~\ref{sec:emergent:map})
but lacks three certificates required for physics-map parity with
Class~II--IV rows:
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Evaluator.} No definition
    $\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ appears in
    \eqref{eq:physics-map-pipeline}; Class~V cites
    $\mathrm{eval}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ only in prose
    (Section~\ref{sec:physics-map:grouping}).
  \item \textbf{Continuum functor.} The replica limit
    \eqref{eq:replica-limit} and Bloch connection
    \eqref{eq:bloch-bands} are Tier~B/C; a proof that
    $\mathcal{E}_N$ converges to a unique continuum effective action
    $S_{\mathrm{eff}}^{\mathrm{cont}}$ on soldered $d=4$ geometry
    (Definition~\ref{def:soldering}) is not yet a theorem.
  \item \textbf{Strong-correlation frontier.}
    Remark~\ref{rmk:emergent-honest} explicitly excludes superconductivity,
    fractional quantum Hall, and other strong-correlation phases; overlap-network
    percolation (Definition~\ref{def:flavon-network}) is not yet tied to
    phase-transition exponents.
  \item \textbf{Quantitative contacts.} Noble-gas closures, Landau parameter
    \eqref{eq:landau-F0}, and free-energy identities are leading-order;
    atomic spectroscopy and quantitative band gaps remain Tier~C imports.
\end{enumerate}
Removing ledger entries \textbf{A5} (flavon truncation) or \textbf{A7} (OS
reconstruction) invalidates subchains but does not affect the void--mirror
climb; Thread~1 upgrades \emph{emergent} rows to explicit
$\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ output without adding primitives.

\paragraph{Wave~2 partial closure (Thread~1).}
The first Class~V domain evaluator, descent factorization for chemistry and
atomic rows, and periodic-tower continuum functor are certified in
Section~\ref{sec:wave2-thread1}
(Definition~\ref{def:thread-1-evaluator},
Theorem~\ref{thm:thread-1-descent},
Definition~\ref{def:thread-1-continuum};
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread-1-wave2-partial}).

\paragraph{Wave~4 Class~V closure (Thread~1).}
QED contact layer, band-gap determinant, critical exponents, stellar opacity
envelope, and nuclear EFT descent from Thread~VI are proved in
Section~\ref{sec:wave4-thread1}
(Corollary~\ref{cor:thread-1-qed},
Theorems~\ref{thm:thread-1-bands},~\ref{thm:thread-1-critical},
Proposition~\ref{prop:thread-1-stellar},
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread-1-closure}).
Residual items---superconductivity, FQHE, biophysics, Navier--Stokes---remain
open per Remark~\ref{rmk:thread1-wave4-table}.

\paragraph{Dependency edges.}
\begin{itemize}[leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Upstream (required).}
    Observer collapse $\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$
    (Definition~\ref{def:heterotic-collapse});
    OS quantum mechanics (Theorem~\ref{thm:qm-derived});
    SM breaking chain (Theorem~\ref{thm:breaking-complete});
    $\sigma$-measure split (Theorem~\ref{thm:sigma-measure}).
  \item \textbf{Peer threads.}
    Thread~2 (weak): induced gravity supplies the background vierbein
    (Proposition~\ref{prop:vierbein}) for continuum limits;
    environmental pressure $\mathcal{P}_{\sigma=+1}$
    (Definition~\ref{def:env-pressure}) enters thermodynamic
    \eqref{eq:thermo-laws}.
    Nuclear/atomic contact (Section~\ref{sec:nuclear-atomic-cosmo}) is a
    \emph{specialization} of Thread~1 at low $N$.
  \item \textbf{Downstream (feeds).}
    Biophysics and plasma rows in Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete};
    precision chemistry and materials Tier~C workbook.
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{Proof-tier upgrade path ($\mathbf{E}\to\mathbf{B}\to\mathbf{A}$).}
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textbf{\arabic*.},leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Tier~E (emergent contact).}
    Current Class~V status: SM\,+\,GR\,+\,QED effective theory with no
    named $\mathcal{F}_D$ (Section~\ref{sec:physics-map:grouping},
    Remark~\ref{rmk:emergent-honest}).
  \item \textbf{Tier~B (ledger-conditional).}
    Close \texttt{def:thread-1-evaluator} and
    \texttt{thm:thread-1-descent} under \textbf{A5} (flavon overlap),
    \textbf{A7} (OS reconstruction for $\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$),
    and \textbf{A8} (environmental pressure routing); matches
    Section~\ref{sec:emergent} tier assignments.
  \item \textbf{Tier~A (void--mirror).}
    Upgrade additivity and locality of $\mathcal{E}_N$
    (Proposition~\ref{prop:emergent-functor}) to a \emph{unique} descent
    functor from $H^1(\mathcal{T}_7,\mathcal{F}_{16})^{\sigma=-1}$ alone,
    eliminating \textbf{A5} from the chemistry ladder
    (Theorem~\ref{thm:chemistry-ladder}) and identifying the replica limit
    with Stone-lift cellular data (Proposition~\ref{prop:stone-lift}) without
    emergent lattice identification.
\end{enumerate}

\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread-1-pipeline}
  \boxed{%
  \begin{aligned}
    \mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}(D)
    \;&=\;
    \mathrm{coarse}_{\beta,N,L}\circ
    \mathcal{E}_N\circ
    \Pi_{\sigma=-1}\circ
    \mathrm{Bal}_{\mathcal{C}}\circ
    \Mirror^{\leq 8}(\Void),\\[4pt]
    \mathcal{E}_N
    \;&=\;
    (\Pi_{\sigma=-1})^{\otimes N},
    \qquad
    \mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}=\mathrm{Im}(\mathcal{E}_N)
    \subset
    \mathcal{H}_{\mathrm{obs}}^{\otimes N}.
  \end{aligned}}
\end{equation}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Thread~2: Strong-curvature and quantum gravity}
\label{sec:thread-2}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

\paragraph{Thread definition.}
\textbf{Thread~2} is the \emph{strong-curvature} route: beyond the
Einstein--Hilbert ledger truncation (\textbf{A1}), where the effective
coupling $\kappa(k)=k^2/\MPl^2(k)$ (Definition~\ref{def:kappa}) reaches the
UV organizing fixed point $\kappa_\star=96\pi^2/5$
(Theorem~\ref{thm:kappa}) and induced $\MPl$ is anchored to the electroweak
scale via Sakharov $a_2$ (Theorem~\ref{thm:planck},
Proposition~\ref{prop:planck-scale}). At curvature scales $R\sim\MPl^2$ and on
black-hole horizons (Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete}, astrophysics row),
the one-loop EH truncation is insufficient; Thread~2 traces how
\emph{higher-curvature} and \emph{graviton} modes are routed to the
$\sigma=+1$ shadow sector (Theorem~\ref{thm:kappa-persistence},
assumption~\textbf{A8}), how dark-matter cohomology residue
$\mathcal{R}_{+1}$ (Definition~\ref{def:dm-residue}) gravitates at
$\kappa_\star$, and how the nonperturbative measure split
\eqref{eq:gamma-split} constrains a horizon EFT \emph{without} importing a
separate quantum-gravity axiom. The target is a named evaluator
$\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{grav}}$ certifying Planck-scale and horizon physics as
outputs of the same void--mirror pipeline.

\centering
\small

  \texttt{thm:thread-2-curvature} (EH domain of validity) \\

  $R^2$, graviton loops, higher curvature &
  Theorem~\ref{thm:kappa-persistence} $\to$

  Absolute Planck mass identification &
  Theorem~\ref{thm:planck}, \eqref{eq:planck-v} $\to$
  \texttt{cor:thread-2-planck} (D3 closure at $\kappa_\star$) \\
QG-BH &
  Black-hole horizons, entropy &

\paragraph{Gap analysis.}
Thread~2 has \textbf{Tier~B} control of $\kappa_\star$ on the observable FRG
row but lacks closed strong-curvature theorems:
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Evaluator.} Black holes appear as
    \emph{Emergent: induced gravity + Tier~B horizon EFT}
    (Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete}) with no
    $\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{grav}}$ definition parallel to
    $\mathcal{F}_{\sigma\mathrm{-split}}$ for cosmology.
  \item \textbf{Horizon certificate.} No theorem identifies observer horizon
    data with $\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$-projected boundary modes on
    $\hat Q$; the Tier~B horizon EFT is named but not derived.
  \item \textbf{Nonperturbative QG.} Theorem~\ref{thm:kappa} is explicitly
    one-loop with higher curvature neglected
    (Section~\ref{sec:physics:gauge}); a nonperturbative fixed-point
    statement for the full gravitational measure on
    $d\mu_{\Gamma_{-1}}\otimes d\mu_{\Gamma_{+1}}$ is not proved.
  \item \textbf{Strong-field $\sigma$ routing.} Theorem~\ref{thm:kappa-persistence}
    treats $R^2$ and graviton loops at the fixed point; explicit strong-curvature
    propagation of $T_{\mu\nu}^{(+1)}$ near horizons is not separated from
    the cosmological shadow residue of Theorem~\ref{thm:dm-sector}.
  \item \textbf{Quantitative contacts.} Planck mass \eqref{eq:planck-v} is
    Tier~B/C (Proposition~\ref{prop:planck-scale}); Bekenstein--Hawking
    entropy and quasi-normal spectra are not in the contact layer.
\end{enumerate}
Thread~2 closes these gaps within the existing ledger
(\textbf{A1},~\textbf{A2},~\textbf{A4},~\textbf{A8}); no new gravitational
primitive is introduced.

\paragraph{Wave~5 partial closure (Thread~2).}
The gravitational evaluator, EH domain, shadow routing, horizon EFT, and
nonperturbative measure are proved in Section~\ref{sec:wave5-thread2}
(Definition~\ref{def:thread-2-evaluator},
Theorems~\ref{thm:thread-2-curvature},~\ref{thm:thread-2-horizon},
~\ref{thm:thread-2-qg};
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread-2-closure}).
See Remark~\ref{rmk:thread2-wave5-table} for post-Wave~5 ledger upgrades.
Residual items: quasi-normal spectra and Tier~A derivation of \textbf{A1}.

\paragraph{Target evaluators and theorems.}
The target bundle
(\texttt{def:thread-2-evaluator} through \texttt{thm:thread-2-qg}) is proved in
Section~\ref{sec:wave5-thread2}; the programme table below records pre-Wave~5
status.

\paragraph{Proof-tier upgrade path ($\mathbf{E}\to\mathbf{B}\to\mathbf{A}$).}

    Current black-hole row: induced gravity + unspecified horizon EFT
    (Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete}); Tier~B/C contact only.
  \item \textbf{Tier~B (ledger-conditional).}
    Close \texttt{def:thread-2-evaluator},
    \texttt{thm:thread-2-horizon}, and
    \texttt{thm:thread-2-qg} under \textbf{A1}--\textbf{A2},
    \textbf{A4}, \textbf{A8}; extend Theorem~\ref{thm:kappa-persistence}
    to strong-field charts $(\tau_\iota,g_\iota)$ along
    Definition~\ref{def:lifetime}.
  \item \textbf{Tier~A (void--mirror).}
    Derive the observer-local EH truncation (\textbf{A1}) from
    $\sigma$-equivariance of \eqref{eq:action} and capacity balance on
    $\mathfrak{m}$ without FRG ledger import; identify
    $\kappa_\star$ as a consequence of the $28|4$ coset split
    (Lemma~\ref{lem:goldstone-sigma}) and anomaly arithmetic
    (Theorem~\ref{thm:beta}) alone; upgrade shadow routing to
    Theorem~\ref{thm:duality} without \textbf{A8} decoupling hypothesis.
\end{enumerate}

\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread-2-pipeline}
  \boxed{%
  \begin{aligned}
    \mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{grav}}(D)
    \;&=\;

    \longmapsto
    \mathcal{M}_{\mathrm{strong}}(D),
    \qquad
    \beta_\kappa\big|_{\sigma=-1,\,\kappa_\star}=0,\\[2pt]
    \beta_{\alpha R^2},\,
    \beta_{\mathrm{graviton}}
    \;&\subset\;
    d\mu_{\Gamma_{+1}}
    \quad
    (\textbf{A8},\ \text{Thm.~\ref{thm:kappa-persistence}}).
  \end{aligned}}
\end{equation}

\begin{remark}[Thread coupling]
\label{rmk:threads-1-2-coupling}
Threads~1 and~2 are logically orthogonal: Thread~1 coarse-grains
$\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$ matter on $\mathcal{T}_7$; Thread~2 organizes
curvature couplings at $\kappa_\star$ and routes strong-field back-reaction
to $d\mu_{\Gamma_{+1}}$. Their intersection is the thermodynamic pressure
term $\mathcal{P}_{\sigma=+1}$ in \eqref{eq:thermo-laws} and the vierbein
(Proposition~\ref{prop:vierbein}) shared by condensed-matter continuum
limits and horizon geometry. Neither thread adds a primitive axiom; both
extend Corollary~\ref{cor:physics-map-closure} with named evaluators
$\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ and $\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{grav}}$.
\end{remark}% --- end 29-threads-1-2.tex ---
% --- 29-threads-3-4.tex ---
%======================================================================%
\section{Research Threads III--IV: Continuum Rigor and Precision Contact}
\label{sec:threads-3-4}
%======================================================================%

Sections~\ref{sec:derivation-complete}--\ref{sec:physics-map} close semantic
coverage of the PDG-aligned physics map. Two \emph{research threads} remain
as explicit programme coordinates: \textbf{Thread~3} (constructive continuum
limit and nonperturbative rigor) and \textbf{Thread~4} (precision and anomaly
contact). This section traces both threads through the same master pipeline
\eqref{eq:master-pipeline}, records open questions in tabular form, names
existing anchors and residual gaps, and states target theorem upgrades with
tier labels and dependency chains. Threads~III and~IV are not new primitives;
they are audit trails for the rigor and precision layers that connect cellular
mirror data to OS quantum mechanics (Thread~3) and to sub-percent PDG contacts
(Thread~4).

%======================================================================%
\subsection{Thread~3: Constructive continuum limit and rigor}
\label{sec:thread-3}
%======================================================================%

\begin{definition}[Thread~3: constructive continuum limit]
\label{def:thread-3}
\emph{Thread~3} is the functorial chain that transports discrete mirror data
on the stabilized Albert tower $\mathcal{T}_7$ to a nonperturbatively
well-defined observer-sector Euclidean measure, then to Lorentzian quantum
mechanics by OS reconstruction. Its pipeline stages are:
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Cellular cohomology} on $\mathcal{T}_7$ with cosheaf
    $\mathcal{F}_{16}$ (Definition~\ref{def:tower7},
    Definition~\ref{def:F16}, Lemma~\ref{lem:cellular}).
  \item \textbf{Profinite Stone lift} to $Q$ with $\sigma$-type stability
    (Proposition~\ref{prop:stone-lift}, Appendix~\ref{sec:appendix:quotient}).
  \item \textbf{Mirror quotient} $\hat Q=Q/\sigma$ and bundle $V_{16}\to\hat Q$
    (Definition~\ref{def:Qhat}, Theorem~\ref{thm:observer-fp}).
  \item \textbf{Radiative mass gap} on the $28$ observer-sector coset
    directions (Theorem~\ref{thm:rp}, assumption~\textbf{A3}).
  \item \textbf{$\sigma$-loop expansion} of the Euclidean measure
    (Theorem~\ref{thm:sigma-measure}, Lemma~\ref{lem:goldstone-sigma}).
  \item \textbf{OS upgrade} from semiclassical reflection positivity to full
    observer-sector reconstruction (Theorems~\ref{thm:rp-gamma-neg},
    \ref{thm:rp-complete}, Proposition~\ref{prop:os-observer},
    Theorem~\ref{thm:qm-derived}).
\end{enumerate}
Thread~3 closes former gap \textbf{P5} (nonperturbative reflection positivity)
and supplies the constructive backbone for Section~\ref{sec:quantum-origin}.
\end{definition}

\paragraph{Existing anchors.}
Thread~3 is already threaded through the manuscript at the following nodes:
\begin{itemize}[leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Cellular $\to$ continuum.}
    Appendix~\ref{sec:appendix:quotient}: triality on $\mathcal{T}_7$
    (Proposition~\ref{prop:triality}), cellular count
    (Lemma~\ref{lem:cellular}), Stone lift
    (Proposition~\ref{prop:stone-lift}), Lefschetz index
    (Theorem~\ref{thm:mirror-index}).
  \item \textbf{Quotient geometry.}
    Definition~\ref{def:Qhat}; observer fixed-point theorem
    (Theorem~\ref{thm:observer-fp}); duality
    (Theorem~\ref{thm:duality}).
  \item \textbf{Mass gap.}
    Coleman--Weinberg gap (Lemma~\ref{lem:breaking-cw}, assumption~\textbf{A3});
    semiclassical RP (Theorem~\ref{thm:rp}); Goldstone split
    (Lemma~\ref{lem:goldstone-sigma}).
  \item \textbf{$\sigma$-measure and loops.}
    Nonperturbative factorization (Theorem~\ref{thm:sigma-measure});
    instanton split parallel (Proposition~\ref{prop:theta-measure});
    graviton/$R^2$ routing (assumption~\textbf{A8},
    Theorem~\ref{thm:kappa-persistence}).
  \item \textbf{OS chain.}
    RP on $d\mu_{\Gamma_{-1}}$ (Theorem~\ref{thm:rp-gamma-neg});
    closure (Theorem~\ref{thm:rp-complete});
    quantum origin (Theorem~\ref{thm:qm-derived},
    Corollary~\ref{cor:qm-origin-closure}).
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{Residual gaps.}
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textbf{G3.\arabic*},leftmargin=*]
  \item \label{gap:thread3-continuum}
    \textbf{Quantitative continuum limit.} Proposition~\ref{prop:stone-lift}
    proves dimensional stability of $H^1$ under profinite refinement; an
    explicit operator-norm bound between cellular and continuum Laplacians on
    $\hat Q$ is not yet recorded.
  \item \label{gap:thread3-sigma-loop}
    \textbf{All-orders $\sigma$-loop expansion.} The tree-level factorization
    \eqref{eq:gamma-split} and one-loop Jacobian block
    (Appendix~\ref{sec:appendix:frg}) are proved; a uniform bound on
    cross-sector loop insertions at order $L\ge 2$ remains a programme item.
  \item \label{gap:thread3-gauge-gap}
    \textbf{Nonperturbative gauge mass gap.} Theorem~\ref{thm:confinement}
    supplies a Tier~C area-law contact; a constructive OS proof for
    $\mathrm{SU}(3)_c$ on $\hat Q$ parallel to Theorem~\ref{thm:rp-complete}
    is not closed.
  \item \label{gap:thread3-a7}
    \textbf{Ledger \textbf{A7} minimization.} Clustering and Euclidean
    symmetry for $d\mu_{\Gamma_{-1}}$ are recorded as a derived truncation
    (Definition~\ref{def:assumption-ledger}, item~\ref{asm:os}); deriving
    \textbf{A7} from void and mirror alone would promote Thread~3 to Tier~A.
\end{enumerate}

\paragraph{Wave~1 closure (Thread~3).}
The quantitative continuum limit, all-orders $\sigma$-loop factorization,
and OS/\textbf{A7} upgrade are proved in Section~\ref{sec:wave1-thread3}
(Theorems~\ref{thm:thread3-continuum}, \ref{thm:thread3-sigma-loop},
\ref{thm:thread3-os-upgrade}; Corollary~\ref{cor:thread3-wave1-closure}).
The coset mass-gap certificate remains in Theorem~\ref{thm:rp}; the sole
residual Thread~3 programme item is the nonperturbative gauge-sector OS gap
(T3-Q9, \ref{gap:thread3-gauge-gap}).

\paragraph{Dependencies and tier upgrades.}
Thread~3 depends on Tier~A inputs (void, mirror, cellular count, triality,
Stone lift) and Tier~B ledger entries \textbf{A3} (Coleman--Weinberg gap),
\textbf{A6} ($\iota$-convexity), \textbf{A7} (OS axioms), and \textbf{A8}
($\sigma$-routed gravity loops). The dependency DAG is
\begin{center}
\small
\begin{tabular}{@{}ll@{}}
\toprule
\textbf{Input} & \textbf{Thread~3 output} \\
\midrule
Lemma~\ref{lem:cellular}, Proposition~\ref{prop:stone-lift} &
  Continuum observer multiplicity \\
Lemma~\ref{lem:breaking-cw}, Theorem~\ref{thm:rp} &
  Coset mass gap \\
Theorem~\ref{thm:sigma-measure}, Lemma~\ref{lem:goldstone-sigma} &
  $\sigma$-loop factorization (tree) \\
Theorem~\ref{thm:rp-gamma-neg}, Proposition~\ref{prop:os-observer} &
  OS reconstruction \\
Theorem~\ref{thm:qm-derived} &
  Quantum mechanics certificate \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabular}
\end{center}
\textbf{Tier upgrades (Wave~1).} \textbf{A7}$\to$\textbf{derived},
cellular stability $\to$ quantitative bound, and P5
(Table~\ref{tab:gap-ledger}) Tier~B$\to$Tier~A are certified in
Section~\ref{sec:wave1-thread3}.

\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread3-pipeline}
  \boxed{%
  \mathcal{T}_7
  \;\xrightarrow{\;\text{Stone}\;}\;
  Q
  \;\xrightarrow{\;/\sigma\;}\;
  \hat Q
  \;\xrightarrow{\;\Pi_{\sigma=-1},\,\mu^2>0\;}\;
  d\mu_{\Gamma_{-1}}
  \;\xrightarrow{\;\text{OS}\;}\;
  \mathcal{H}_{\mathrm{obs}}
  }
\end{equation}
Equation~\eqref{eq:thread3-pipeline} is the Thread~3 specialization of
\eqref{eq:master-pipeline} to the rigor layer; Section~\ref{sec:quantum-origin}
records the OS endpoint (Corollary~\ref{cor:qm-origin-closure}).

%======================================================================%
\subsection{Thread~4: Precision and anomaly contact}
\label{sec:thread-4}
%======================================================================%

\begin{definition}[Thread~4: precision and anomaly contact]
\label{def:thread-4}
\emph{Thread~4} is the experimental contact thread: Tier~A anomaly arithmetic
and $\beta$-function identities propagate through the ledger FRG and two-loop
threshold matching to sub-percent PDG observables, CP-odd invariants, and
hadronic residues. Its stages are:
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Anomaly anchor.} Cubic and mixed anomaly cancellation
    (Theorem~\ref{thm:anomaly}); $b_0=12$ from $\mathbf{27}$ content
    (Theorem~\ref{thm:beta}).
  \item \textbf{Ledger FRG.} Extended Jacobian
    (Proposition~\ref{prop:frg-jacobian}, Appendix~\ref{sec:appendix:frg});
    capacity residues $\mathcal{R}_\iota(\mu)$ on observer charts.
  \item \textbf{Two-loop thresholds.} Flavon, Yukawa, electroweak, and QCD
    refinements (Theorems~\ref{thm:nu-ratio-2loop},
    \ref{thm:quark-mass-2loop}, Theorem~\ref{thm:g2-2loop}).
  \item \textbf{Precision closure.} Definition~\ref{def:tier-c-closure};
    Corollaries~\ref{cor:tier-c-closure},~\ref{cor:quark-tier-c}.
  \item \textbf{CP phases.} CKM $(\rho,\eta)$ from $\mathcal{P}_{ij}$
    (Proposition~\ref{prop:ckm-precision}); strong CP
    (Theorem~\ref{thm:strong-cp}); baryogenesis
    (Proposition~\ref{prop:flavon-cp}).
\end{enumerate}
Thread~4 closes the D1--D3 precision programme and extends semantic closure
(Corollary~\ref{cor:semantic-closure}) to quark and hadron sectors.
\end{definition}

\paragraph{Existing anchors.}
Thread~4 is anchored at:
\begin{itemize}[leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Tier~A anomaly sector.}
    Theorem~\ref{thm:anomaly} (cubic $16-80+64=0$, mixed $-1$);

  \item \textbf{Flavour precision.}

    $\Delta a_\mu$, $\sin^2\theta_W(M_Z)$
    (Table~\ref{tab:tier-c-precision},
    Table~\ref{tab:predictions-comparison}).
  \item \textbf{Quark sector.}

    Proposition~\ref{prop:ckm-precision}, Prediction~\ref{pred:ckm-pdg};

  \item \textbf{Validation ledger.}
    Table~\ref{tab:experimental-validation};
    Definition~\ref{def:contact-map};
    Corollary~\ref{cor:tier-c-closure}.
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{Residual gaps.}
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textbf{G4.\arabic*},leftmargin=*]
  \item \label{gap:thread4-alpha-s}
    \textbf{Strong coupling.} One-loop residue \eqref{eq:alpha-s-mz} overshoots
    PDG by $\sim 15\%$; two-loop remark in Section~\ref{sec:qcd:alpha-s} is
    not yet a closed theorem.
  \item \label{gap:thread4-hadrons}
    \textbf{Hadron spectrum.} \emph{Resolved in Wave~2}
    (Section~\ref{sec:wave2-thread4},
    Theorem~\ref{thm:thread4-hadron-precision},
    Corollary~\ref{cor:thread4-wave2-closure}).
  \item \label{gap:thread4-Vub}
    \textbf{$|V_{ub}|$ tail.} Table~\ref{tab:ckm-pdg}: $|V_{ub}|$ at $\sim 6\%$
    tolerance, the weakest CKM entry.
  \item \label{gap:thread4-jarlskog}
    \textbf{Jarlskog invariant.} $(\rho,\eta)$ are closed individually; a
    single derived $J_{\mathrm{CKM}}$ from imaginary parts of
    $\mathcal{P}_{ij}$ is not yet recorded.
  \item \label{gap:thread4-anomaly-two-loop}
    \textbf{Two-loop anomaly matching.} Tier~A one-loop identities are exact;
    threshold corrections to $b_0$ and GS coefficients at GUT scales are not
    tabulated.
\end{enumerate}

\paragraph{Wave~1 partial closure (Thread~4).}

are proved in Section~\ref{sec:wave1-thread4}
(Theorems~\ref{thm:thread4-alpha-s}, \ref{thm:thread4-cp-phases},
\ref{thm:thread4-anomaly-contact}; Corollary~\ref{cor:thread4-wave1-partial}).
Hadron precision is closed in Wave~2 (Section~\ref{sec:wave2-thread4},
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread4-wave2-closure}); the residual Thread~4 item is
$|V_{ub}|$ (\ref{gap:thread4-Vub}).

\paragraph{Wave~2 hadron closure (Thread~4).}

Corollary~\ref{cor:thread4-wave2-closure} refine
Prediction~\ref{pred:hadron-masses} with two-loop
$\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}^{(2)}\approx 0.34\,\mathrm{GeV}$ and triality overlap
phases from Theorem~\ref{thm:thread4-cp-phases}, closing
\ref{gap:thread4-hadrons} and merging Thread~4 with
Section~\ref{sec:qcd:hadrons}.

%======================================================================%
\subsection{Thread coupling and programme status}
\label{sec:threads-3-4-coupling}
%======================================================================%

Threads~3 and~4 are not independent. Thread~3 supplies the measure and OS
foundation on which Thread~4 loop arithmetic is defined: capacity residues
$\mathcal{R}_\iota$ are observer-chart functionals
(Remark~\ref{rmk:observer-frg}); $\sigma$-loop factorization
(Theorem~\ref{thm:sigma-measure}) ensures that precision observables computed
in $d\mu_{\Gamma_{-1}}$ are not contaminated by shadow-sector normalization;
the Coleman--Weinberg gap (Theorem~\ref{thm:rp}) sets the scale
$\mu\equiv v$ (Proposition~\ref{prop:mu-lifetime}) used in every Thread~4
workbook. Conversely, Thread~4 validates Thread~3: the $b_0=12$ anchor enters
the mass-gap counting on coset scalars ($n_S=28$); anomaly cancellation
guarantees that OS-reconstructed gauge dynamics is consistent at the contact
layer.

\begin{table}[ht]
\centering
\small
\renewcommand{\arraystretch}{1.12}
\begin{tabular}{@{}llll@{}}
\toprule
\textbf{Thread} & \textbf{Closed items} & \textbf{Open targets} & \textbf{Tier} \\
\midrule
3 &
  Cellular $\to$ $\hat Q$; coset mass gap; continuum bound;
  all-orders $\sigma$-split; Tier~A OS (\ref{cor:thread3-wave1-closure}) &
  Gauge-sector nonperturbative gap (T3-Q9) &
  A \\
4 &
  $b_0$, GS; $\Delta m^2$, $m_\mu/m_e$, $g$-2, CKM, strong CP;
  Jarlskog (\ref{cor:thread4-wave1-partial}) &
  Thms.~\ref{thm:thread4-alpha-s},~\ref{thm:thread4-hadron-precision};
  $|V_{ub}|$ &
  A/C \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabular}
\caption{Thread~3--4 programme status as of mid-2026. \textbf{Closed} rows
cite proved manuscript content; \textbf{Open targets} name the upgrade
theorems of this section.}
\label{tab:threads-3-4-status}
\end{table}

\begin{corollary}[Thread audit certificate]\label{cor:threads-3-4-audit}
Relative to the semantic closure certificate
(Corollary~\ref{cor:semantic-closure}):
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item Thread~3 has \textbf{eight} of nine questions closed
    (Table~\ref{tab:thread-3-questions}); Wave~1
    (Section~\ref{sec:wave1-thread3},
    Corollary~\ref{cor:thread3-wave1-closure}) closed T3-Q6--Q8; the sole
    residual item is the gauge-sector nonperturbative OS gap (T3-Q9).
  \item Thread~4 has \textbf{nine} of eleven questions closed;
    Wave~1 partial closure (Section~\ref{sec:wave1-thread4},
    Corollary~\ref{cor:thread4-wave1-partial}) records Jarlskog/CP-phase
    upgrade; residual items are $\alpha_s(M_Z)$, hadron masses, and
    $|V_{ub}|$.
  \item No thread introduces a new primitive: both are audit trails over
    \eqref{eq:master-pipeline} with tier upgrades explicitly named.
\end{enumerate}
\end{corollary}

\begin{remark}[Wave~1 closure sections]
Thread~3 Wave~1 proofs and the closure certificate
(Corollary~\ref{cor:thread3-wave1-closure}) are recorded in
Section~\ref{sec:wave1-thread3}. Thread~4 partial Wave~1 upgrade
(Corollary~\ref{cor:thread4-wave1-partial}) is recorded in
Section~\ref{sec:wave1-thread4}. The question ledgers above cite these
sections for rows closed in Wave~1.
\end{remark}

\begin{remark}[Relation to physics map]
Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete} Class~II (dynamical, Tier~B) and
Class~III (flavour and precision, Tier~C) are the physics-map avatar of
Threads~3 and~4 respectively. Corollary~\ref{cor:physics-map-closure}
therefore subsumes the closed portions of this section; the thread tables
record what remains for full Tier~A OS derivation and sub-percent QCD/hadron
contact.
\end{remark}% --- end 29-threads-3-4.tex ---
% --- 29-threads-5-6.tex ---
%======================================================================%
\section{Development Threads V--VI: Cosmological Perturbations and
Hadron--Nuclear Spectroscopy}
\label{sec:threads-5-6}
%======================================================================%

Threads~V and~VI extend the master physics map
(Section~\ref{sec:physics-map}) from \emph{background} cosmology and
\emph{leading} hadronic contacts to the perturbative and spectroscopic
functors required for CMB anisotropies, large-scale structure, and the
full low-energy mass ladder. Both threads are \textbf{descent layers} on the
same pipeline \eqref{eq:physics-map-pipeline}; neither introduces a primitive
beyond $(\Void,\Mirror)$. Thread~III (SM Lagrangian certificate,
Section~\ref{sec:sm-lagrangian}) and Thread~IV (cosmological background
ledger, Sections~\ref{sec:dark-sector},~\ref{sec:cosmology},
~\ref{sec:baryogenesis}) supply the transport inputs $(v,\eta_B,\alpha_{\mathrm{em}},
\Omega_{\mathrm{DM}},H_0^{\mathrm{CMB}},\mathcal{P}_{\sigma=+1})$ that
Threads~V and~VI consume.

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Thread~5: Cosmological perturbations}
\label{sec:thread-5}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

Cosmological \emph{background} quantities---$\Omega_{\mathrm{DM}}$,
$H_0^{\mathrm{CMB}}$, $w(z)\approx -1$, $\eta_B$---are closed in
Threads~III--IV. Thread~V records the \textbf{perturbation functor}: how
$\sigma$-split stress--energy and capacity weights propagate into density
contrasts, growth, and CMB/LSS observables.

\begin{definition}[Thread~5: capacity-graded cosmological perturbation]
\label{def:thread5-pert}
Fix the homogeneous background of Theorems~\ref{thm:hubble-cmb},
~\ref{thm:dm-abundance}, and Prediction~\ref{pred:cc}. Let
$\delta_{\sigma=\pm1}(\mathbf{x},\tau)$ denote the density contrast in the
$\sigma$-graded stress--energy split \eqref{eq:T-split} about
$\orderparam_\star$. The \emph{Thread~5 perturbation datum} is the pair
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-datum}
  \boldsymbol{\delta}
  \;:=\;
  \bigl(
    \delta_{(-1)},\,\delta_{(+1)},\,D_\pm(z),\,P_\pm(k),\,n_s,\,\sigma_8
  \bigr),
\end{equation}
where $\delta_{(-1)}$ is supported on observable baryon--radiation modes in
$H^1(\hat Q,V_{16})^{\sigma=-1}$, $\delta_{(+1)}$ on the mirror-shadow
residue $\mathcal{R}_{+1}$ (Definition~\ref{def:dm-residue}), $D_\pm$ are
linear growth factors in each sector, $P_\pm$ the corresponding matter power
spectra, and $(n_s,\sigma_8)$ the scalar tilt and late-time fluctuation
amplitude contacted in Prediction~\ref{pred:cmb} and
Proposition~\ref{prop:sigma8}.
\end{definition}

\centering
\small

\begin{tabular}{@{}p{0.30\linewidth}p{0.58\linewidth}@{}}

\midrule
What sources primordial scalar perturbations without an inflation postulate? &
  Coleman--Weinberg gap on $28$ coset scalars

  ledger Jacobian tilt gives $n_s\neq 1$
  (\eqref{eq:pred-ns}). \textbf{Open:} full curvature perturbation
  $\mathcal{R}$ from $\orderparam$ fluctuations. \\
\addlinespace
How do $\sigma=+1$ shadow modes cluster without observable interactions? &
  Theorem~\ref{thm:dm-sector} identifies $\rho_{\mathrm{DM}}$;
  Proposition~\ref{prop:sigma8} fixes $\sigma_8$ from capacity ratio
  $\sqrt{(w_1+w_2)/w_3}$. \textbf{Open:} non-linear
  $\delta_{(+1)}$ beyond linear growth. \\
\addlinespace
What is the matter power spectrum $P(k)$ at sub-percent accuracy? &
  Leading $P(k)\propto k^{n_s-1}$ with $n_s$ from
  \eqref{eq:pred-ns}. \textbf{Open:} two-loop acoustic peak locations;
  Silk damping from atomic sector
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:atomic-spectrum}). \\

  (Proposition~\ref{prop:hz-ledger}). \textbf{Closed} at linear order. \\

  No tensor postulate in SJET. \textbf{Open:} $\sigma$-even graviton
  residue routed to $d\mu_{\Gamma_{+1}}$
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:kappa-persistence}) as hidden tensor ledger. \\

\paragraph{SJET anchors.}
Thread~5 is anchored on the following proved or contacted chain:
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{$\sigma$-sector stress split.}
    $T_{\mu\nu}=T_{\mu\nu}^{(-1)}+T_{\mu\nu}^{(+1)}$
    (Theorem~\ref{thm:dm-sector}, \eqref{eq:T-split}).
  \item \textbf{Environmental vacuum ledger.}
    $\mathcal{P}_{\sigma=+1}$ and CMB Friedmann constraint
    (Definition~\ref{def:env-pressure}, \eqref{eq:friedmann-cmb}).
  \item \textbf{Shadow abundance and clustering.}
    $\Omega_{\mathrm{DM}}=4/15$ (Theorem~\ref{thm:dm-abundance});
    $\sigma_8=\sqrt{11/16}$ (Proposition~\ref{prop:sigma8}).
  \item \textbf{Baryon sector.}
    $\eta_B\approx 6\times 10^{-10}$ (Theorem~\ref{thm:baryogenesis});
    $\Omega_b h^2$ (Prediction~\ref{pred:cmb}, \eqref{eq:pred-omega-b}).
  \item \textbf{Scalar tilt.}
    $n_s=1-(w_2/w_3)(b_0-n_F)/\kappa_\star$ (Prediction~\ref{pred:cmb},
    \eqref{eq:pred-ns}).
  \item \textbf{Hubble anchors.}
    Theorems~\ref{thm:hubble-local},~\ref{thm:hubble-cmb};
    DESI $H(z)$ contact (Prediction~\ref{pred:hz}).
\end{enumerate}

\paragraph{Gaps.}
Thread~5 does \textbf{not} yet supply:
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Partially closed (Wave~2--3).}
    The linear two-fluid Boltzmann hierarchy
    \eqref{eq:thread5-growth}--\eqref{eq:thread5-kstar} is derived in
    Section~\ref{sec:wave2-thread5}; one-loop non-linear $P(k)$ and halo mass
    function are in Section~\ref{sec:wave3-thread5}; full curvature
    perturbation $\mathcal{R}$ and two-loop peaks remain open.
  \item \textbf{Partially closed (Wave~3).}
    Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-nl-power} and
    Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-press-schechter} supply leading non-linear
    observables; sub-percent refinement remains Tier~C.
  \item CMB lensing amplitude $A_L$ and full acoustic peak spectrum at
    Planck precision.
  \item Tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$ from the $\sigma=+1$ graviton reservoir.
\end{enumerate}
These are Tier~C refinement targets (Section~\ref{sec:tier-c-precision}), not
epistemic primitives.

\paragraph{Wave~2 partial closure (Thread~5).}
The capacity two-fluid growth system, perturbation ledger identities, and
leading matter power spectrum with first acoustic scale $k_\star$ are proved in
Section~\ref{sec:wave2-thread5}
(Theorems~\ref{thm:thread5-target},~\ref{prop:thread5-ledger},
~\ref{thm:thread5-power}; Corollary~\ref{cor:thread5-wave2-closure}).

\paragraph{Wave~3 non-linear closure (Thread~5).}
Shadow-sector screening, Press--Schechter halo mass function, and one-loop
$P_{(-1)}^{\mathrm{nl}}(k)$ are proved in Section~\ref{sec:wave3-thread5}
(Lemma~\ref{lem:thread5-shadow-nl},
Theorems~\ref{thm:thread5-press-schechter},~\ref{thm:thread5-nl-power};
Corollary~\ref{cor:thread5-wave3-closure}).
Residual items are CMB lensing $A_L$ and tensor ratio $r$.

\paragraph{Target functor $\mathcal{F}_D$ and theorems.}
The Thread~5 evaluator is
\begin{equation}\label{eq:FD-cosmo-pert}
  \mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{cosmo\text{-}pert}}
  \;:=\;
  \mathrm{eval}_{\sigma\text{-}\mathrm{pert}}
  \;:\;
  \mathbf{Struct}\times\mathbf{Ledger}
  \longrightarrow

\end{equation}
with $\mathbf{PertObs}$ the contact layer
$(\delta_\pm,P_\pm,n_s,\sigma_8,f\sigma_8,\Omega_b h^2)$.
The target theorem bundle
(\texttt{thm:thread5-target}, \texttt{prop:thread5-ledger},
\texttt{thm:thread5-power}) is proved in Section~\ref{sec:wave2-thread5}
(Theorems~\ref{thm:thread5-target},~\ref{prop:thread5-ledger},

The programme table below records pre-Wave~2 status; see

  }
\end{equation}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Thread~6: Hadron and nuclear spectroscopy functor}
\label{sec:thread-6}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

Thread~VI closes the \textbf{nonperturbative spectroscopy} route from
cellular overlap data on $\mathcal{T}_7$ to hadron masses, nuclear binding
ladders, and atomic/CMB transport contacts. Yukawa overlaps
(Section~\ref{sec:yukawa}) fix perturbative quark masses; QCD confinement
(Section~\ref{sec:qcd}) and nuclear--cosmology mapping
(Section~\ref{sec:nuclear-atomic-cosmo}) supply the leading spectroscopic
contacts.

\begin{definition}[Thread~6: spectroscopy evaluator]
\label{def:thread6-spec}
Let $\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}$ be the confinement scale of
Definition~\ref{def:lambda-qcd} (equivalently Proposition~\ref{prop:alpha-s},
\eqref{eq:Lambda-QCD}). For each colour-singlet hadron $H$ with constituent
slots $(i,j,k)$ on $\mathcal{T}_7$, let $\mathcal{A}_H$ be the hadronic
overlap of Definition~\ref{def:hadron-overlap}. For each nucleus with mass
number $A$, let $\mathcal{N}_A$ denote the $A$-fold nuclear overlap
(Definition~\ref{def:nuclear-overlap}, Theorem~\ref{thm:nuclear-binding}).
The \emph{Thread~6 spectroscopy datum} is
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread6-datum}
  \boldsymbol{\mathcal{S}}
  \;:=\;
  \Bigl\{
    m_H=\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}\,|\mathcal{A}_H|^{1/n_q}
  \Bigr\}_{H\in\mathcal{H}}
  \;\cup\;
  \Bigl\{
    E_B(A)/A=\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}\,\tfrac{w_2}{w_3 b_0}\,\mathcal{F}(A)
  \Bigr\}_{A\in\mathbb{N}}.
\end{equation}
\end{definition}

\begin{table}[ht]
\centering
\small
\renewcommand{\arraystretch}{1.12}
\begin{tabular}{@{}p{0.30\linewidth}p{0.58\linewidth}@{}}
\toprule
\textbf{Unanswered question} & \textbf{SJET status / residual work} \\
\midrule
What fixes the hadron mass spectrum beyond the proton and pion? &
  Definition~\ref{def:hadron-overlap} and
  Lemma~\ref{lem:hadron-cellular} reduce masses to hub triple
  intersections; Prediction~\ref{pred:hadron-masses} contacts
  $m_p$, $m_\pi$, $m_\rho$. \textbf{Open:} full PDG baryon/meson table. \\
\addlinespace
Why do nuclear magic numbers include $28=n_S$? &
  Theorem~\ref{thm:nuclear-binding}: shell closures at
  $A_\star\in\{2,8,20,28\}$ from $28$ coset scalars
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:planck}). \textbf{Closed} at leading order. \\
\addlinespace
What is the binding energy per nucleon at the iron peak? &
  \eqref{eq:binding-peak}: $\max E_B/A\approx 11$\,MeV from
  $\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}w_2/(w_3 b_0)$. \textbf{Open:} two-body and
  three-body force refinements ($\mathcal{O}(20\%)$). \\
\addlinespace
How does $\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}$ enter without a separate confinement axiom? &
  Definition~\ref{def:lambda-qcd} from $n_F=3$ and $\alpha_s(M_Z)$;
  Proposition~\ref{prop:alpha-s} from ledger FRG. \textbf{Closed}. \\
\addlinespace
What links hadronic scales to BBN and CMB? &
  Section~\ref{sec:nuclear-atomic-cosmo}: deuteron gate
  \eqref{eq:deuteron-binding}, $Y_p$, $D/H$, $T_{\mathrm{CMB}}$,
  $\Omega_b h^2$. \textbf{Closed} at Tier~B/C. \\
\addlinespace
Can excited resonances and Regge trajectories be derived? &
  \textbf{Open:} $\iota=2$ excitation ansatz in \eqref{eq:mrho-pred};
  no Regge functor yet. \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabular}
