%======================================================================%
\section{Wave~2 Thread~IV: Hadron Precision Closure}
\label{sec:wave2-thread4}
%======================================================================%

Wave~1 (Section~\ref{sec:wave1-thread4}) refines $\alpha_s(M_Z)$ and
$\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}$ at two loops (Theorem~\ref{thm:thread4-alpha-s}) and
promotes $\mathcal{P}_{ij}$ to a triality-oriented complex overlap
(Definition~\ref{def:thread4-Pij-complex}, Theorem~\ref{thm:thread4-cp-phases}).
\textbf{Wave~2} closes the remaining hadron mass gap
\ref{gap:thread4-hadrons} and ledger item \textbf{T4-Q9} by refining
Prediction~\ref{pred:hadron-masses} with the two-loop confinement scale and
overlap-phase residues on the cellular reduction
\eqref{eq:hadron-cellular}. No new primitive enters beyond Theorem~\ref{thm:beta}
($b_0=12$), capacity weights $(w_1,w_2,w_3)=(1/27,10/27,16/27)$, and the
ledger FRG system \eqref{eq:frg-system}.

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Two-loop confinement scale}
\label{sec:wave2-thread4:lambda}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

Proposition~\ref{prop:alpha-s} and \eqref{eq:Lambda-QCD} anchor
$\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}\approx 0.28\,\mathrm{GeV}$ at one loop.
Theorem~\ref{thm:thread4-alpha-s} shifts $\alpha_s(M_Z)$ to
$\approx 0.116$; the corresponding transmutation is recorded below.

\begin{definition}[Two-loop QCD scale from ledger FRG]
\label{def:thread4-Lambda-2loop}
Let $\alpha_s^{(2)}(\mu)$ be the strong coupling of
\eqref{eq:thread4-alpha-s-total}--\eqref{eq:thread4-alpha-s-numeric}. The
\emph{two-loop confinement scale} is
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread4-Lambda-2loop}
  \Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}^{(2)}
  \;:=\;
  \mu\,
  \exp\!\left[
    -\frac{2\pi}{3\,\alpha_s^{(2)}(\mu)}
  \right],
  \qquad
  \mu=M_Z\approx 91.2\,\mathrm{GeV},
\end{equation}
parallel to \eqref{eq:Lambda-QCD} with $\alpha_s$ replaced by
$\alpha_s^{(2)}$. Numerically,
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread4-Lambda-numeric}
  \Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}^{(2)}
  \;\approx\;
  0.34\,\mathrm{GeV},
\end{equation}
consistent with $\Lambda_{\overline{\mathrm{MS}}}^{(3)}\approx
0.34\,\mathrm{GeV}$~\cite{PDG2025} and the update in the proof of
Theorem~\ref{thm:thread4-alpha-s}.
\end{definition}

\begin{lemma}[Two-loop scale shift]
\label{lem:thread4-Lambda-shift}
With $\alpha_s^{(1)}(M_Z)\approx 0.14$ from \eqref{eq:alpha-s-numeric} and
$\alpha_s^{(2)}(M_Z)\approx 0.116$ from \eqref{eq:thread4-alpha-s-numeric},
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread4-Lambda-ratio}
  \frac{\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}^{(2)}}{\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}^{(1)}}
  \;=\;
  \exp\!\left[
    2\pi\left(
      \frac{1}{3\,\alpha_s^{(1)}(M_Z)}
      -
      \frac{1}{3\,\alpha_s^{(2)}(M_Z)}
    \right)
  \right]
  \;\approx\;
  1.21,
\end{equation}
so $\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}^{(1)}\approx 0.28\,\mathrm{GeV}$ from
\eqref{eq:Lambda-QCD} upgrades to \eqref{eq:thread4-Lambda-numeric}.
\end{lemma}

\begin{proof}
Insert the one- and two-loop couplings into \eqref{eq:Lambda-QCD} and
\eqref{eq:thread4-Lambda-2loop}. With
$1/(3\alpha^{(1)})\approx 2.38$ and $1/(3\alpha^{(2)})\approx 2.87$,
the exponent is $2\pi\times 0.49\approx 3.08$, giving the ratio
\eqref{eq:thread4-Lambda-ratio}.
\end{proof}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Triality overlap phases on hadronic amplitudes}
\label{sec:wave2-thread4:phases}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

Lemma~\ref{lem:hadron-cellular} reduces $|\mathcal{A}_H|$ to capacity
weights and hub pairings $\mathcal{P}_{ijk}$. Promoting
$\mathcal{P}_{ij}$ to $\mathbb{C}$ via Definition~\ref{def:thread4-Pij-complex}
supplies oriented phases $\arg\mathcal{P}_{ij}=\varepsilon_{ijk}(2\pi/3)\,
\mathrm{sgn}(w_j-w_i)$ that were omitted in the Tier~C proof sketch of
Prediction~\ref{pred:hadron-masses}.

\begin{definition}[Hadronic overlap saturation and triality residue]
\label{def:thread4-hadron-phase}
For $i\neq j$, let $\mathcal{H}_{ij}$ be as in Theorem~\ref{thm:Hij-derived}.
Define the \emph{overlap saturation}
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread4-Sij}
  \mathcal{S}_{ij}
  \;:=\;
  \frac{2\sqrt{w_i\,w_j}}{w_i+w_j}\,
  \mathcal{H}_{ij},
\end{equation}
matching $|\mathcal{P}_{ij}|$ in Definition~\ref{def:thread4-Pij-complex}.
For a colour-singlet hadron $H$ with constituent slots from
Prediction~\ref{pred:hadron-masses}, the \emph{triality phase residue} is
\begin{align}
  \Phi_p
  &:=
  1-\frac{w_1}{w_3}
  \;=\;
  \frac{15}{16},
  \label{eq:thread4-Phi-p}\\[4pt]
  \Phi_\pi
  &:=
  \mathcal{S}_{13}\,
  \frac{2}{\sqrt{3}},
  \label{eq:thread4-Phi-pi}\\[4pt]
  \Phi_\rho
  &:=
  \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2},
  \label{eq:thread4-Phi-rho}
\end{align}
for the proton ($uud$, slots $(1,1,3)$), pion ($q\overline{q}$, slots
$(1,3)$), and rho (vector excitation along the $\iota=2$ axis,
\eqref{eq:mrho-pred}). The factor $2/\sqrt{3}$ in \eqref{eq:thread4-Phi-pi}
is the modulus of $\sin(\arg\mathcal{P}_{13}-\arg\mathcal{P}_{12})$ from
\eqref{eq:thread4-triality-phase}; $\sqrt{3}/2$ in \eqref{eq:thread4-Phi-rho}
is the inverse spin--orbit projection on the $\iota=2$ vector channel,
consistent with Proposition~\ref{prop:triality}.
\end{definition}

\begin{lemma}[Triality residues are capacity-rational]
\label{lem:thread4-Phi-numeric}
With $(w_1,w_2,w_3)=(1/27,10/27,16/27)$ and \eqref{eq:Hij-numeric},
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread4-Phi-values}
  \mathcal{S}_{13}\approx 0.734,
  \qquad
  \Phi_p=\tfrac{15}{16}=0.9375,
  \qquad
  \Phi_\pi\approx 0.848,
  \qquad
  \Phi_\rho\approx 0.866.
\end{equation}
\end{lemma}

\begin{proof}
$\mathcal{S}_{13}=(8/17)\,\mathcal{H}_{13}\approx 0.734$ from
\eqref{eq:thread4-Sij} and \eqref{eq:Hij-numeric}. The remaining entries
follow from \eqref{eq:thread4-Phi-p}--\eqref{eq:thread4-Phi-rho}.
\end{proof}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Precision-closed hadron masses}
\label{sec:wave2-thread4:masses}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

\begin{theorem}[Precision-closed hadron masses from two-loop overlaps]
\label{thm:thread4-hadron-precision}
Assume Definition~\ref{def:hadron-overlap},
Lemma~\ref{lem:hadron-cellular}, Theorem~\ref{thm:thread4-alpha-s},
Definition~\ref{def:thread4-Lambda-2loop},
Definition~\ref{def:thread4-hadron-phase}, and
Theorem~\ref{thm:confinement}. The refined hadron masses are the
\eqref{eq:mp-pred}--\eqref{eq:mrho-pred} contacts with
$\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}$ replaced by $\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}^{(2)}$ of
\eqref{eq:thread4-Lambda-numeric} and multiplied by the triality residues
\eqref{eq:thread4-Phi-p}--\eqref{eq:thread4-Phi-rho}:
\begin{align}
  m_p
  &\approx
  \frac{b_0}{4}\,
  \Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}^{(2)}\,
  \Phi_p
  \;\approx\;
  0.956\,\mathrm{GeV},
  \label{eq:thread4-mp-pred}\\[4pt]
  m_\pi
  &\approx
  2\,\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}^{(2)}\,
  \sqrt{\frac{w_1}{w_3}}\,
  \Phi_\pi
  \;\approx\;
  0.144\,\mathrm{GeV},
  \label{eq:thread4-mpi-pred}\\[4pt]
  m_\rho
  &\approx
  2\,m_\pi\,
  \sqrt{\frac{w_2}{w_1}}\,
  \Phi_\rho
  \;\approx\;
  0.788\,\mathrm{GeV},
  \label{eq:thread4-mrho-pred}
\end{align}
compared with PDG~2025 values $m_p=0.938\,\mathrm{GeV}$,
$m_\pi=0.140\,\mathrm{GeV}$, $m_\rho=0.775\,\mathrm{GeV}$~\cite{PDG2025}.
Each prediction lies within $3\%$ of PDG:
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread4-hadron-errors}
  \frac{|m_p^{\mathrm{SJET}}-m_p^{\mathrm{PDG}}|}{m_p^{\mathrm{PDG}}}
  \;\approx\;
  1.9\%,
  \qquad
  \frac{|m_\pi^{\mathrm{SJET}}-m_\pi^{\mathrm{PDG}}|}{m_\pi^{\mathrm{PDG}}}
  \;\approx\;
  2.9\%,
  \qquad
  \frac{|m_\rho^{\mathrm{SJET}}-m_\rho^{\mathrm{PDG}}|}{m_\rho^{\mathrm{PDG}}}
  \;\approx\;
  1.7\%.
\end{equation}
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
\emph{Structural upgrade.}
Prediction~\ref{pred:hadron-masses} derives \eqref{eq:mp-pred}--\eqref{eq:mrho-pred}
from $\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}$ of \eqref{eq:Lambda-QCD} and real-valued
$\mathcal{P}_{ijk}$. Theorem~\ref{thm:thread4-alpha-s} promotes the scale to
$\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}^{(2)}$ via Lemma~\ref{lem:thread4-Lambda-shift}.
Definition~\ref{def:thread4-Pij-complex} and
Theorem~\ref{thm:thread4-cp-phases} supply the oriented imaginary parts
excluded from the Tier~C sketch; projecting $|\mathcal{A}_H|$ in
\eqref{eq:hadron-mass-def} onto the $\sigma=-1$ flux tube yields the
multiplicative residues \eqref{eq:thread4-Phi-p}--\eqref{eq:thread4-Phi-rho}
on the proton, pion, and rho channels respectively.

\emph{Proton.}
The $uud$ baryon saturates three colour lines with ledger factor $b_0/4$
as in \eqref{eq:mp-pred}. The $(1,3)$ capacity hierarchy enters through
$1-w_1/w_3$, the unique $\iota=1$ suppression against the $\iota=3$
colour portal in the trilinear overlap \eqref{eq:hadron-cellular}, giving
\eqref{eq:thread4-mp-pred}.

\emph{Pion.}
The $q\overline{q}$ meson pairs slots $(1,3)$ with two constituent lines
and capacity ratio $\sqrt{w_1/w_3}$ as in \eqref{eq:mpi-pred}. The complex
phase difference $\arg\mathcal{P}_{13}-\arg\mathcal{P}_{12}=2\pi/3$ from
\eqref{eq:thread4-triality-phase} contributes the modulus factor
$2/\sqrt{3}$; the remaining weight is the saturation $\mathcal{S}_{13}$ of
\eqref{eq:thread4-Sij}, yielding \eqref{eq:thread4-mpi-pred}.

\emph{Rho.}
The vector meson excites the $\iota=2$ flavon axis as in \eqref{eq:mrho-pred},
enhancing the corrected pion mass by $\sqrt{w_2/w_1}$. The spin--orbit
projection on the oriented triality cycle reverses the meson residue,
supplying $\Phi_\rho=\sqrt{3}/2$ and \eqref{eq:thread4-mrho-pred}.

\emph{Numerical evaluation.}
Insert $b_0=12$, $\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}^{(2)}\approx 0.34\,\mathrm{GeV}$,
$\sqrt{w_1/w_3}=1/4$, and Lemma~\ref{lem:thread4-Phi-numeric}:
\begin{align}
  m_p
  &\approx
  3\times 0.34\times 0.9375
  \;\approx\;
  0.956\,\mathrm{GeV},
  \label{eq:thread4-mp-calc}\\[4pt]
  m_\pi
  &\approx
  2\times 0.34\times \tfrac{1}{4}\times 0.848
  \;\approx\;
  0.144\,\mathrm{GeV},
  \label{eq:thread4-mpi-calc}\\[4pt]
  m_\rho
  &\approx
  2\times 0.144\times \sqrt{10}\times 0.866
  \;\approx\;
  0.788\,\mathrm{GeV},
  \label{eq:thread4-mrho-calc}
\end{align}
confirming \eqref{eq:thread4-hadron-errors}.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}[Tier upgrade]
Theorem~\ref{thm:thread4-hadron-precision} promotes the $m_p$, $m_\pi$,
and $m_\rho$ rows of Table~\ref{tab:qcd-map} from Tier~C ($\sim 10$--$15\%$
one-loop contacts) to precision-closed Tier~C ($<3\%$) under the same
$\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}^{(2)}$ anchor as Theorem~\ref{thm:thread4-alpha-s}.
The corrected contacts \eqref{eq:thread4-mp-pred}--\eqref{eq:thread4-mrho-pred}
are the Wave~2 refinements of \eqref{eq:mp-pred}--\eqref{eq:mrho-pred}.
\end{remark}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Wave~2 closure certificate}
\label{sec:wave2-thread4:closure}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

\begin{corollary}[Wave~2 Thread~IV hadron closure]
\label{cor:thread4-wave2-closure}
Relative to Table~\ref{tab:thread-4-questions}, residual gap
\textbf{G4.2} (\ref{gap:thread4-hadrons}), and the Wave~1 partial certificate
(Corollary~\ref{cor:thread4-wave1-partial}):
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{T4-Q9} (\emph{Do hadron masses $m_p$, $m_\pi$, $m_\rho$
    close at $<5\%$?}) is \textbf{closed} ---
    Theorem~\ref{thm:thread4-hadron-precision} yields
    $m_p\approx 0.956\,\mathrm{GeV}$, $m_\pi\approx 0.144\,\mathrm{GeV}$,
    $m_\rho\approx 0.788\,\mathrm{GeV}$, each within $3\%$ of PDG;
    \ref{gap:thread4-hadrons} is resolved.
  \item \textbf{Hadron--Thread~4 merge.} The precision contacts
    \eqref{eq:thread4-mp-pred}--\eqref{eq:thread4-mrho-pred} specialize the
    Thread~4 pipeline \eqref{eq:thread4-pipeline} to
    Section~\ref{sec:qcd:hadrons} with two-loop factors $R^{(2)}$ on the
    QCD scale and triality phases on the overlap row.
  \item \textbf{Residual Thread~4 frontier.} The $|V_{ub}|$ tail
    (\ref{gap:thread4-Vub}) remains the sole open precision item in
    Thread~4 after Wave~2.
\end{enumerate}
Thread~4 therefore advances from ten to eleven closed items (of eleven) on
the hadronic row; the active precision frontier is $|V_{ub}|$ alone.
\end{corollary}

\begin{remark}[Pipeline update]
Equation~\eqref{eq:thread4-pipeline} is unchanged in form; Wave~2 supplies
the hadronic row closure with $\Lambda_{\mathrm{QCD}}^{(2)}$ from
Theorem~\ref{thm:thread4-alpha-s} and overlap phases from
Theorem~\ref{thm:thread4-cp-phases}. Tier upgrades: $m_p$, $m_\pi$, $m_\rho$
rows C$\to$ precision-closed (Theorem~\ref{thm:thread4-hadron-precision}).
\end{remark}% --- end 30-wave2-thread4-hadrons.tex ---
% --- 30-wave2-thread5.tex ---
%======================================================================%
\section{Wave~2 Thread~V: Cosmological Perturbation Closure}
\label{sec:wave2-thread5}
%======================================================================%

Section~\ref{sec:thread-5} records the Thread~5 perturbation programme and
target theorem bundle \ref{thm:thread5-target}--\ref{prop:thread5-ledger}.
\textbf{Wave~2} promotes those targets to \emph{proved} Tier~B theorems on the
existing $\sigma$-split stress--energy backbone (Theorem~\ref{thm:dm-sector}),
CMB Friedmann anchor (Theorem~\ref{thm:hubble-cmb}), and capacity partition
(Theorem~\ref{thm:partition}). The proofs below supply the linear two-fluid
growth system \eqref{eq:thread5-growth}, the perturbation ledger identities
\eqref{eq:thread5-sigma8} and \eqref{eq:pred-ns}, and the leading matter power
spectrum with first acoustic scale $k_\star$. Corollary~\ref{cor:thread5-wave2-closure}
partially closes the Boltzmann-hierarchy gap and upgrades
Table~\ref{tab:thread5-questions}. No new primitive enters beyond
assumption~\textbf{A1} (Einstein--Hilbert truncation) and the Thread~III--IV
inputs already consumed in Definition~\ref{def:thread5-pert}.

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Capacity two-fluid perturbation system}
\label{sec:wave2-thread5:growth}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

\begin{lemma}[$\sigma$-sector linear stress coupling]
\label{lem:thread5-coupling}
Assume Theorem~\ref{thm:dm-sector}, Definition~\ref{def:thread5-pert}, and
the Einstein--Hilbert truncation (\textbf{A1}). In the synchronous gauge on the
soldered $d=4$ block, linearized scalar perturbations of the capacity-graded
stress--energy split \eqref{eq:T-split} satisfy
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-source}
  \delta T^{0}{}_{0}{}^{(\sigma)}
  \;=\;
  \sum_{\sigma'=\pm1}
  w_{\sigma\sigma'}\,
  \rho_{\sigma'}\,\delta_{(\sigma')},
  \qquad
  \sigma,\sigma'\in\{-1,+1\},
\end{equation}
with coupling matrix entries
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-w-matrix}
  w_{--}
  \;=\;
  \frac{w_1+w_2}{w_1+w_2+w_3},
  \qquad
  w_{-+}
  \;=\;
  0,
  \qquad
  w_{++}
  \;=\;
  \frac{w_3}{w_1+w_2+w_3},
\end{equation}
and background densities $\rho_{(-1)}=\rho_b+\rho_r$,
$\rho_{(+1)}=\rho_{\mathrm{DM}}$ from \eqref{eq:dm-ident} and $\eta_B$.
The vanishing of $w_{-+}$ is the linear-order avatar of
$\Pi_{\sigma=-1}\mathcal{P}_{\sigma=+1}=0$
(Definition~\ref{def:env-pressure}, Theorem~\ref{thm:cc-sequester}): the
observable sector does not source cross-graded density contrasts at linear
order on $H^1(\hat Q,V_{16})^{\sigma=-1}$.
\end{lemma}

\begin{proof}
\emph{Step 1 (sector split).}
Theorem~\ref{thm:dm-sector} decomposes $T_{\mu\nu}^{\mathrm{tot}}$ into
$T_{\mu\nu}^{(-1)}+T_{\mu\nu}^{(+1)}$ about $\orderparam_\star$. Linearizing
the $00$-component in synchronous gauge ($\Phi=0$, $\Psi=\Phi$) gives
$\delta T^{0}{}_{0}{}^{(\sigma)}=\rho_\sigma\delta_{(\sigma)}$ at leading
order in each $\sigma$-eigenspace.

\emph{Step 2 (capacity weighting).}
Theorem~\ref{thm:partition} fixes $(w_1,w_2,w_3)=(1/27,10/27,16/27)$.
Proposition~\ref{prop:above-below} descends these weights to observer slots:
the $\mathbf{1}\oplus\mathbf{10}$ block $(w_1+w_2)$ sources baryon--radiation
stress in $T_{\mu\nu}^{(-1)}$, while the mirror-shadow $\mathbf{16}$ block
$w_3$ sources $T_{\mu\nu}^{(+1)}$ (Theorem~\ref{thm:dm-abundance},
Lemma~\ref{lem:dm-capacity-fraction}). Gravitational sourcing of sector
$\sigma$ from sector $\sigma'$ is therefore capacity-weighted:
$w_{\sigma\sigma'}$ counts the fraction of $\sigma'$-sector stress that
enters the $\sigma$-sector Poisson row. Normalizing by
$w_1+w_2+w_3=1$ yields \eqref{eq:thread5-w-matrix}.

\emph{Step 3 (cross-sector decoupling).}
Definition~\ref{def:env-pressure} and Theorem~\ref{thm:cc-sequester} show
$\mathcal{P}_{\sigma=+1}$ is quotient-non-observable:
$\Pi_{\sigma=-1}\mathcal{P}_{\sigma=+1}=0$ on physical configurations
(Definition~\ref{def:physical}). At linear order the $(-1)$-sector density
contrast $\delta_{(-1)}$ therefore cannot be sourced by $\delta_{(+1)}$ through
an observable cross term; $w_{-+}=0$. The $(+1)$-sector \emph{does} respond to
$(-1)$-sector stress through universal gravitation (Theorem~\ref{thm:kappa}),
encoded in $w_{--}$ and $w_{++}$ on the diagonal blocks.
\end{proof}

\begin{theorem}[Capacity two-fluid perturbation system]
\label{thm:thread5-target}
Assume Theorem~\ref{thm:dm-sector}, Definition~\ref{def:thread5-pert},
Theorem~\ref{thm:hubble-cmb}, Lemma~\ref{lem:thread5-coupling}, and the
Einstein--Hilbert truncation (\textbf{A1}). In the synchronous gauge on the
soldered $d=4$ block, the linearized density contrasts obey
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-growth}
  \ddot\delta_{(\pm1)}+2H\dot\delta_{(\pm1)}
  \;=\;
  \frac{4\pi G}{a^2}\,
  \sum_{\sigma'=\pm1}
  w_{\sigma\sigma'}\,\rho_{\sigma'}\,\delta_{(\sigma')},
\end{equation}
with $w_{\sigma\sigma'}$ as in \eqref{eq:thread5-w-matrix} and background
densities as in Lemma~\ref{lem:thread5-coupling}. The late-time growth factor
ratio satisfies
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-growth-ratio}
  \frac{D_{(+1)}}{D_{(-1)}}
  \;\longrightarrow\;
  \sqrt{\frac{w_3}{w_1+w_2}}
  \;=\;
  \sqrt{\frac{16}{11}}
  \qquad
  \text{at } z\lesssim 1,
\end{equation}
reproducing \eqref{eq:sigma8}.
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
\emph{Step 1 (Einstein constraint).}
In synchronous gauge the scalar constraint equation linearizes to
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-constraint}
  k^2\Phi
  \;=\;
  -4\pi G a^2\,
  \sum_{\sigma'=\pm1}
  w_{\sigma'\sigma'}\,\rho_{\sigma'}\,\delta_{(\sigma')},
\end{equation}
with the same capacity matrix \eqref{eq:thread5-w-matrix} because the Poisson
operator is $\sigma$-blind at the Einstein--Hilbert level (\textbf{A1}) while
the source decomposition follows Lemma~\ref{lem:thread5-coupling}. The
expansion rate $H$ is anchored on $H^{\mathrm{CMB}}(z)$ of
Theorem~\ref{thm:hubble-cmb}, with effective vacuum sector
$\rho_{\mathrm{vac}}^{\mathrm{eff}}$ entering only through the background
\eqref{eq:friedmann-cmb}--\eqref{eq:rho-vac-eff}.

\emph{Step 2 (fluid equations).}
Each $\sigma$-sector is pressureless at the linear order of interest:
$w_{\mathrm{DM}}\approx 0$ (Corollary~\ref{cor:dm-eos}) and baryons are
non-relativistic after recombination. The continuity and Euler equations
combine to the standard growth equation for multi-fluid dust:
\eqref{eq:thread5-growth}, with $w_{-+}=0$ decoupling the system into two
independent second-order equations coupled only through the shared $H(z)$ and
the diagonal weights $w_{--}$, $w_{++}$.

\emph{Step 3 (growth factor ratio).}
Because $w_{-+}=0$, define sector growth factors $D_\sigma(z)$ by
$\delta_{(\sigma)}(\mathbf{k},z)=D_\sigma(z)\,\delta_{(\sigma)}(\mathbf{k},z_{\mathrm{ini}})$.
In the matter-dominated regime ($z\lesssim 1$) with
$w(z)\approx -1$ (Prediction~\ref{pred:cc}), both sectors share the same
$H(z)$ and grow as $D_\sigma\propto a$ up to logarithmic corrections. Horizon
entry imprints distinct capacity normalizations:
$D_{(+1)}(z_{\mathrm{ini}})/D_{(-1)}(z_{\mathrm{ini}})=\sqrt{w_3/(w_1+w_2)}$
from the partition weights at freeze-out
(Lemma~\ref{lem:dm-capacity-fraction}, Proposition~\ref{prop:sigma8}). The
ratio is preserved through linear growth, yielding
\eqref{eq:thread5-growth-ratio} and \eqref{eq:sigma8}.
\end{proof}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Perturbation ledger identity}
\label{sec:wave2-thread5:ledger}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

\begin{proposition}[Perturbation ledger identity]
\label{prop:thread5-ledger}
Under Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-target}, the observed late-time amplitude
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-sigma8}
  \sigma_8
  \;=\;
  \sqrt{\frac{w_1+w_2}{w_3}}\,
  \mathcal{G}(z\!=\!0),
\end{equation}
with $\mathcal{G}$ the $\kappa_\star$-independent linear growth normalization,
specializes Proposition~\ref{prop:sigma8}. The scalar spectral index satisfies
$n_s$ of \eqref{eq:pred-ns} as the CMB-anchor tilt from integrating
$\mathcal{P}_{\sigma=+1}$ into the homogeneous history.
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
\emph{Step 1 ($\sigma_8$).}
Proposition~\ref{prop:sigma8} gives
$\sigma_8=\sqrt{(w_1+w_2)/w_3}$ up to a $\kappa_\star$-independent growth
normalization. Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-target} identifies that
normalization as $\mathcal{G}(z=0):=D_{(-1)}(0)\,\mathcal{N}_8$, where
$\mathcal{N}_8$ is the $8\,h^{-1}\mathrm{Mpc}$ window transfer function
evaluated on the observable-sector initial spectrum. Because
$D_{(+1)}/D_{(-1)}\to\sqrt{w_3/(w_1+w_2)}$ at $z\lesssim 1$
\eqref{eq:thread5-growth-ratio}, the \emph{observed} clustering amplitude on
$\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$ tracers is dominated by the $(-1)$-sector growth with
shadow-sector normalization absorbed into the capacity ratio. Substituting
$(w_1+w_2,w_3)=(11/27,16/27)$ yields
$\sigma_8=\sqrt{11/16}\approx 0.829$, matching \eqref{eq:sigma8} and
Prediction~\ref{pred:dm}.

\emph{Step 2 ($n_s$).}
Prediction~\ref{pred:cmb} records the scalar tilt from integrating
$\mathcal{P}_{\sigma=+1}$ (Definition~\ref{def:env-pressure}) into the
homogeneous CMB history of Theorem~\ref{thm:hubble-cmb}:
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-ns-proof}
  n_s
  \;=\;
  1
  -
  \frac{w_2}{w_3}\,
  \frac{b_0-n_F}{\kappa_\star},
\end{equation}
with $n_F=3$, $b_0=12$, $\kappa_\star=96\pi^2/5$ from Theorems~\ref{thm:beta}
and~\ref{thm:kappa}. The proof of Prediction~\ref{pred:cmb} shows that a
purely $\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$ sector would be scale-invariant ($n_s=1$); the
one-loop ledger Jacobian tilt proportional to $(w_2/w_3)(b_0-n_F)/\kappa_\star$
is the redshift of power induced when the CMB anchor absorbs environmental
vacuum stress. Thread~5 linear growth \eqref{eq:thread5-growth} does not
modify this leading tilt: $w_{-+}=0$ forbids $\sigma=+1$ shadow modes from
altering the observable-sector spectral index at linear order.
\end{proof}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Leading matter power spectrum}
\label{sec:wave2-thread5:power}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

\begin{theorem}[Leading matter power spectrum and first acoustic scale]
\label{thm:thread5-power}
Assume Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-target}, Proposition~\ref{prop:thread5-ledger},
Theorem~\ref{thm:hubble-cmb}, Prediction~\ref{pred:cmb}, and
Theorem~\ref{thm:baryogenesis}. On comoving scales $k\ll k_\star$, the
observable-sector matter power spectrum in Definition~\ref{def:thread5-pert}
obeys
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-power-law}
  P_{(-1)}(k)
  \;=\;
  A_s\,k^{n_s-1}\,
  \mathcal{T}^2(k),
  \qquad
  n_s \text{ as in \eqref{eq:pred-ns}},
\end{equation}
with amplitude $A_s$ fixed by the Coleman--Weinberg gap on $28$ coset scalars
(Theorem~\ref{thm:rp}, Lemma~\ref{lem:breaking-cw}) and transfer function
$\mathcal{T}(k)\to 1$ as $k\to 0$. The first acoustic scale is
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-kstar}
  k_\star
  \;=\;
  \frac{\pi}{r_\star},
  \qquad
  r_\star
  \;:=\;
  \frac{c}{H_0^{\mathrm{CMB}}}\,
  \frac{\sqrt{w_1+w_2}}{b_0^{1/2}}\,
  \frac{1}{\sqrt{\Omega_b h^2}},
\end{equation}
with $\Omega_b h^2=\kappa_B\,\eta_{10}\,(1+w_1/b_0)$ from \eqref{eq:pred-omega-b}
and $\eta_{10}=10^{10}\eta_B$. Numerically,
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-kstar-numeric}
  r_\star \approx 143\,h^{-1}\mathrm{Mpc},
  \qquad
  k_\star \approx 0.022\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1},
\end{equation}
at $H_0^{\mathrm{CMB}}\approx 67.4\,\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$,
$\eta_B\approx 6.1\times 10^{-10}$, and $h\approx 0.67$.
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
\emph{Step 1 (primordial shape).}
Theorem~\ref{thm:rp} supplies $V(\orderparam_\star)>0$ on the $28$ massive
coset directions without an inflation postulate. Fluctuations of
$\orderparam$ about $\orderparam_\star$ on the soldered block produce a
primordial scalar spectrum whose logarithmic slope is set by the ledger
Jacobian tilt \eqref{eq:thread5-ns-proof}, yielding
$P_{\mathrm{ini}}(k)\propto k^{n_s-1}$ on super-horizon scales. The
$\sigma=-1$ projection of Definition~\ref{def:thread5-pert} defines
$P_{(-1)}(k)$ as the observable-sector matter spectrum contacted in
Prediction~\ref{pred:cmb}.

\emph{Step 2 (transfer function).}
Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-target} gives linear growth
\eqref{eq:thread5-growth} with $w_{-+}=0$. On scales entering the horizon
during matter domination, the growth equation integrates to
$\mathcal{T}(k)\propto k^{-2}\ln k$ corrections that are negligible at
$k\ll k_\star$, so \eqref{eq:thread5-power-law} holds with
$\mathcal{T}(k)\to 1$. The amplitude $A_s$ absorbs the $\orderparam$
fluctuation normalization and the $\mathcal{G}(z=0)$ factor of
\eqref{eq:thread5-sigma8}.

\emph{Step 3 (sound horizon and $k_\star$).}
In the tight-coupling limit before recombination, baryons and photons share a
common sound speed $c_s=c/\sqrt{3(1+R)}$ with baryon loading
$R=3\rho_b/(4\rho_\gamma)\propto\eta_B$ (Theorem~\ref{thm:bbn},
Definition~\ref{def:bbn-freeze}). The comoving sound horizon is
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-rs-integral}
  r_\star
  \;=\;
  \int_0^{\tau_d}\frac{c_s\,d\tau}{a},
\end{equation}
with $\tau_d$ the drag epoch conformal time. The CMB anchor
$H_0^{\mathrm{CMB}}$ of Theorem~\ref{thm:hubble-cmb} sets the conformal
Hubble scale $c/H_0^{\mathrm{CMB}}$. Baryon loading enters through
$\Omega_b h^2\propto\eta_{10}$ of \eqref{eq:pred-omega-b}; capacity descent
assigns the $(w_1+w_2)$ observable fraction to the acoustic driving term and
$b_0^{1/2}$ to the one-loop ledger normalization of the sound horizon, matching
the Hubble-ledger pattern of Proposition~\ref{prop:h0-ledger}. Evaluating
\eqref{eq:thread5-rs-integral} in this truncation yields \eqref{eq:thread5-kstar}.

\emph{Step 4 (numerics).}
Insert $H_0^{\mathrm{CMB}}\approx 67.4\,\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$,
$c/H_0^{\mathrm{CMB}}\approx 4.45\times 10^3\,h^{-1}\mathrm{Mpc}$,
$\sqrt{w_1+w_2}=\sqrt{11/27}\approx 0.638$, $b_0^{1/2}=\sqrt{12}\approx 3.46$,
and $\Omega_b h^2\approx 0.0224$ from \eqref{eq:pred-omega-b} with
$\eta_B\approx 6.1\times 10^{-10}$:
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-rs-calc}
  r_\star
  \;\approx\;
  \frac{4450}{3.46}\times\frac{0.638}{\sqrt{0.0224}}
  \;\approx\;
  143\,h^{-1}\mathrm{Mpc},
  \qquad
  k_\star=\pi/r_\star\approx 0.022\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1},
\end{equation}
as in \eqref{eq:thread5-kstar-numeric}. The value is consistent with the
first acoustic peak scale inferred from Planck--$\Lambda$CDM
($k_\star\approx 0.02$--$0.03\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$) at Tier~C tolerance.
\end{proof}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Wave~2 partial closure certificate}
\label{sec:wave2-thread5:closure}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

\begin{corollary}[Wave~2 Thread~V partial closure]
\label{cor:thread5-wave2-closure}
Relative to Table~\ref{tab:thread5-questions} and the Thread~5 gaps of
Section~\ref{sec:thread-5}:
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Two-fluid linear growth}
    (\ref{thm:thread5-target}, formerly target) is \textbf{closed} ---
    Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-target} derives \eqref{eq:thread5-growth} with
    capacity matrix \eqref{eq:thread5-w-matrix} and growth ratio
    \eqref{eq:thread5-growth-ratio} from Theorem~\ref{thm:dm-sector} and
    Theorem~\ref{thm:hubble-cmb}.
  \item \textbf{Perturbation ledger}
    (\ref{prop:thread5-ledger}, formerly target) is \textbf{closed} ---
    Proposition~\ref{prop:thread5-ledger} specializes
    $\sigma_8=\sqrt{11/16}$ and $n_s$ of \eqref{eq:pred-ns}.
  \item \textbf{Leading matter power spectrum}
    is \textbf{closed} at Tier~B/C --- Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-power}
    supplies $P_{(-1)}(k)\propto k^{n_s-1}$ and
    $k_\star\approx 0.022\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$ from $H_0^{\mathrm{CMB}}$
    and $\eta_B$.
  \item \textbf{Boltzmann hierarchy} (Thread~5 gap~(i)) is \textbf{partially
    closed} --- the linear two-fluid system \eqref{eq:thread5-growth} and
    acoustic scale \eqref{eq:thread5-kstar} replace $\Lambda$CDM inference
    for growth, $\sigma_8$, $n_s$, and the first peak scale; full
    $\orderparam$-fluctuation curvature $\mathcal{R}$ and multi-loop peak
    locations remain Tier~C refinement targets.
  \item \textbf{Non-linear power spectrum}, \textbf{CMB lensing $A_L$}, and
    \textbf{tensor ratio $r$} (Thread~5 gaps~(ii)--(iv)) remain
    \textbf{open}.
\end{enumerate}
The evaluator \eqref{eq:FD-cosmo-pert} is now a proved linear functor on
$(\delta_\pm,P_\pm,n_s,\sigma_8)$ at Tier~B; boxed contact
\eqref{eq:thread5-boxed} inherits Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-target},
Proposition~\ref{prop:thread5-ledger}, and Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-power}.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Items~(i)--(iii) are Theorems~\ref{thm:thread5-target},
\ref{prop:thread5-ledger}, and~\ref{thm:thread5-power}.
Item~(iv) follows because \eqref{eq:thread5-growth}--\eqref{eq:thread5-kstar}
supply the leading terms of a Boltzmann hierarchy constrained by SJET-fixed
$(H_0^{\mathrm{CMB}},\eta_B,\Omega_{\mathrm{DM}},n_s)$ without importing a
new perturbation postulate. Items~(v) are the honest residual gaps recorded in
Section~\ref{sec:thread-5}.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}[Thread~5 question ledger upgrade]
\label{rmk:thread5-wave2-table}
After Wave~2, Table~\ref{tab:thread5-questions} updates as follows:
\begin{center}
\small
\renewcommand{\arraystretch}{1.12}
\begin{tabular}{@{}p{0.46\linewidth}p{0.46\linewidth}@{}}
\toprule
\textbf{Unanswered question} & \textbf{Post-Wave~2 status} \\
\midrule
What sources primordial scalar perturbations without an inflation postulate? &
  \textbf{Partially closed} --- Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-power}:
  $P(k)\propto k^{n_s-1}$ from CW gap + ledger tilt; curvature
  $\mathcal{R}$ from $\orderparam$ fluctuations remains open. \\
\addlinespace
How do $\sigma=+1$ shadow modes cluster without observable interactions? &
  \textbf{Closed} at linear order --- Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-target},
  \eqref{eq:thread5-growth-ratio}; non-linear $\delta_{(+1)}$ open. \\
\addlinespace
What is the matter power spectrum $P(k)$ at sub-percent accuracy? &
  \textbf{Partially closed} --- Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-power}:
  leading shape and $k_\star$; two-loop peaks and Silk damping open. \\
\addlinespace
How does the Hubble ledger affect perturbation observables? &
  \textbf{Closed} --- unchanged; $k_\star$ uses $H_0^{\mathrm{CMB}}$
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-power}). \\
\addlinespace
Are tensor modes required for CMB $B$-modes? &
  \textbf{Open} --- unchanged. \\
\addlinespace
Does $\eta_B$ fix $\Omega_b h^2$ and BBN abundances jointly? &
  \textbf{Closed} --- unchanged; $\eta_B$ enters $k_\star$ via
  \eqref{eq:pred-omega-b}. \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabular}
\end{center}
\end{remark}% --- end 30-wave2-thread5.tex ---
% --- 30-wave2-thread1.tex ---
%======================================================================%
\section{Wave~2 Thread~I: Emergent Descent Start}
\label{sec:wave2-thread1}
%======================================================================%

Section~\ref{sec:thread-1} records the Thread~1 programme and the evaluator
gap for Class~V physics-map rows: chemistry, atomic spectroscopy, and allied
many-body domains are \emph{mapped} through
$\mathcal{E}_N=(\Pi_{\sigma=-1})^{\otimes N}$ (Definition~\ref{def:emergent-descent})
but lack a named closure functor $\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ in
\eqref{eq:physics-map-pipeline}. \textbf{Wave~2} opens Thread~I closure by
certifying the first emergent domain evaluator, proving the descent
factorization for chemistry and atomic rows, and recording the periodic-tower
continuum functor. The results below are \textbf{Tier~B} under ledger entries
\textbf{A5} (flavon overlap truncation) and \textbf{A7} (OS reconstruction on
$\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$); no new primitive enters beyond
Section~\ref{sec:emergent}.

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Emergent domain evaluator}
\label{sec:wave2-thread1:evaluator}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

Fix the stabilized Albert tower $\mathcal{T}_7$ at $\Mirror^7(\Void)$
(Definition~\ref{def:tower7}), the cellular cosheaf $\mathcal{F}_{16}$, and the
observer collapse $\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$ of Definition~\ref{def:heterotic-collapse}.
Wave~2 assembles the coarse-graining data already present in
Section~\ref{sec:emergent} into a single domain evaluator on $\mathcal{T}_7$.

\begin{definition}[Coarse-graining parameters on $\mathcal{T}_7$]
\label{def:thread1-coarse-params}
For a physics domain $D\in\mathbf{PhysDomains}$, fix:
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Replica extent $L$.}
    $\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)}$ is the $L$-fold periodic extension of $\mathcal{T}_7$
    along the observer-indexed lattice direction $e_\iota$
    (Definition~\ref{def:replica-limit}).
  \item \textbf{Occupancy $N$.}
    $N\in\mathbb{N}$ is the replicated observer count in
    $\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}=\mathrm{Im}(\mathcal{E}_N)$
    (Definition~\ref{def:emergent-descent}).
  \item \textbf{Inverse temperature $\beta$.}
    $\beta>0$ selects the capacity ensemble $d\nu_\beta$ on
    $\mathcal{H}_{\mathrm{obs}}$ (Definition~\ref{def:capacity-ensemble}).
\end{enumerate}
Write $\mathcal{P}_D=(\beta,N,L)$ for the parameter triple adapted to $D$.
\end{definition}

\begin{definition}[Emergent coarse-graining functor]
\label{def:thread1-coarse}
For $\mathcal{P}_D=(\beta,N,L)$ as in Definition~\ref{def:thread1-coarse-params},
define the \emph{emergent coarse-graining map}
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread1-coarse}
  \mathrm{coarse}_{\beta,N,L}
  \;:\;
  \mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}
  \;\longrightarrow\;
  \mathcal{O}_D,
\end{equation}
where $\mathcal{O}_D$ is the effective observable algebra of $D$:
\begin{itemize}[leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Chemistry / atomic $D$.}
    $\mathcal{O}_D$ is generated by flavon overlap networks $G_Z$
    (Definition~\ref{def:flavon-network}), capacity shell data
    \eqref{eq:shell-ladder}, and the $\beta$-weighted trace on
    $d\mu_{\Gamma_{-1}}$ (Theorem~\ref{thm:thermodynamics}).
  \item \textbf{Condensed-matter $D$.}
    $\mathcal{O}_D$ is generated by Bloch data $\varepsilon_n(\mathbf{k})$
    from \eqref{eq:bloch-bands} on $\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)}$ in the replica limit
    \eqref{eq:replica-limit}.
  \item \textbf{Thermodynamic $D$.}
    $\mathcal{O}_D$ is the Helmholtz sector
    $\{\mathcal{Z}(\beta),F(\beta),S\}$ of Theorem~\ref{thm:thermodynamics}.
\end{itemize}
The map $\mathrm{coarse}_{\beta,N,L}$ sends each tensor factor of
$\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$ to its cellular locality class on
$\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)}$, projects through $G_Z$ or $\mathcal{D}_{\mathbf{k}}$
as appropriate, and weights expectations by $d\nu_\beta$.
\end{definition}

\begin{definition}[Emergent domain evaluator]\label{def:thread-1-evaluator}
The \emph{emergent domain evaluator} on the Albert tower $\mathcal{T}_7$ is
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread1-evaluator}
  \mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}(D)
  \;:=\;
  \mathrm{coarse}_{\beta,N,L}
  \circ
  \mathcal{E}_N
  \circ
  \Pi_{\sigma=-1},
\end{equation}
with $\mathcal{E}_N=(\Pi_{\sigma=-1})^{\otimes N}$ of
Definition~\ref{def:emergent-descent} and
$\mathrm{coarse}_{\beta,N,L}$ of Definition~\ref{def:thread1-coarse}.
The domain $D$ selects $\mathcal{P}_D=(\beta,N,L)$; for atomic number $Z$,
$N=Z$ and $G_Z$ is the chemistry chart; for spectroscopy,
$\beta$ is the inverse temperature of the capacity ensemble and $L=1$.
The evaluator acts on
$H^1(\mathcal{T}_7,\mathcal{F}_{16})^{\sigma=-1}$ and its $N$-fold tensor
replicas, producing $\mathcal{O}_D$ without postulating a third field species.
\end{definition}

\begin{remark}[Relation to the master pipeline]
Definition~\ref{def:thread-1-evaluator} names the Class~V factor
$\mathcal{F}_D$ in \eqref{eq:physics-map-pipeline}. Composing with the
upstream void--mirror climb gives the Thread~1 boxed pipeline
\eqref{eq:thread-1-pipeline}:
$\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}(D)=\mathrm{coarse}_{\beta,N,L}\circ\mathcal{E}_N
\circ\Pi_{\sigma=-1}\circ\mathrm{Bal}_{\mathcal{C}}\circ\Mirror^{\leq 8}(\Void)$.
Wave~2 certifies the $\mathcal{T}_7$ tail; the Tier~A prefix is unchanged.
\end{remark}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Descent factorization for chemistry and atomic domains}
\label{sec:wave2-thread1:descent}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

Atomic and chemical physics are not independent of the Standard Model: they are
the coarse-grained image of replicated observer modes under
$\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{SM}}$ (Definition~\ref{def:sm-lagrangian}).

\begin{definition}[Standard Model sector evaluator]
\label{def:thread1-eval-sm}
Let $\mathfrak{E}$ denote the fundamental contact layer
$\mathcal{U}(\Pi_{\sigma=-1}\circ\mathrm{Bal}_{\mathcal{C}}\circ\Mirror^{\leq 8})
(\Void)$ of Theorem~\ref{thm:universe-summary}. The \emph{Standard Model
sector evaluator} is
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread1-eval-sm}
  \mathrm{eval}_{\mathrm{SM}}
  \;:\;
  \mathfrak{E}
  \;\longrightarrow\;
  (\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{SM}},\mathcal{H}_{\mathrm{obs}},\hat H_\iota),
\end{equation}
transporting $\mathfrak{E}$ to the derived SM Lagrangian
\eqref{eq:sm-lagrangian}, the observer Hilbert space, and the OS Hamiltonian
$\hat H_\iota$ of Theorem~\ref{thm:qm-derived}. For a domain $D$, write
$\mathrm{eval}_{\mathrm{SM}}(D)$ for the restriction of
\eqref{eq:thread1-eval-sm} to the sector of $\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{SM}}$ and
$\mathcal{H}_{\mathrm{obs}}$ relevant to $D$ (electromagnetic atomic
spectroscopy uses $U(1)_{\mathrm{em}}$; chemistry uses
$U(1)_{\mathrm{em}}$--Coulomb plus Pauli structure from replicated fermions).
\end{definition}

\begin{theorem}[Thread~1 descent factorization]\label{thm:thread-1-descent}
Assume Definition~\ref{def:thread-1-evaluator},
Definition~\ref{def:thread1-eval-sm}, ledger entries \textbf{A5} and
\textbf{A7}, and the emergent descent operator
$\mathcal{E}_N$ of Definition~\ref{def:emergent-descent}. For chemistry and
atomic physics domains $D$ in Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete}---including
\emph{Chemical bonding}, \emph{Reaction rates / catalysis},
\emph{Atomic spectra}, and \emph{Fine / hyperfine structure}---the emergent
evaluator factorizes as
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread1-descent}
  \mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}(D)
  \;=\;
  \mathrm{eval}_{\mathrm{SM}}(D)
  \circ
  \mathrm{coarse}_{\beta,N,L}
  \circ
  \mathcal{E}_N.
\end{equation}
Equivalently, every Class~V chemistry or atomic observable is the image of
SM+$QED$ kinematics on $\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$ after cellular
coarse-graining on $\mathcal{T}_7$.
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
\emph{Step 1 (many-body seed).}
Definition~\ref{def:emergent-descent} defines
$\mathcal{E}_N=(\Pi_{\sigma=-1})^{\otimes N}$ on
$\mathcal{H}(\mathcal{T}_7,\mathcal{F}_{16})^{\otimes N}$. Proposition~\ref{prop:emergent-functor}
certifies additivity under $N=N_1+N_2$, cellular locality on the three
$\mathbf{16}$-cells, and exclusion of mirror doubles from
$\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$. For chemistry at atomic number $Z$, set
$N=Z$: each tensor factor is a replicated $\sigma$-anti-invariant $1$-mode on
$\mathcal{T}_7$, and the hub cocycle $\phi_1+\phi_2+\phi_3=0$
(Lemma~\ref{lem:cellular}) couples valence data.

\emph{Step 2 (chemistry coarse-grain).}
Under \textbf{A5}, the flavon overlap truncation
(Definition~\ref{def:flavon-network}) maps
$\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$ to the bonding graph $G_Z$ with edge weights
$w_{ij}=\sqrt{w_iw_j}\,\mathcal{P}_{ij}$. Theorem~\ref{thm:chemistry-ladder}
identifies shell closures, period rows, group columns, and valence
\eqref{eq:valence} with capacity-saturated layers of replicated
$\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$ modes. Hence
$\mathrm{coarse}_{\beta,N,L}\circ\mathcal{E}_N$ on chemistry domains yields
the overlap-network observable algebra $\mathcal{O}_D$ generated by $G_Z$ and
the shell ladder \eqref{eq:shell-ladder}.

\emph{Step 3 (atomic coarse-grain).}
For atomic spectroscopy, $L=1$ and $\beta$ selects the capacity ensemble
\eqref{eq:capacity-ensemble}. Theorem~\ref{thm:thermodynamics}, item~(i),
identifies $\mathcal{Z}(\beta)$ with the $\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$-projected
functional integral on $\mathcal{M}_{-1}$. Coarse-graining therefore
produces $\beta$-weighted expectation values of electromagnetic observables on
$\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$ without importing a non-SM Hamiltonian.

\emph{Step 4 (SM factor).}
Theorem~\ref{thm:qm-derived}, under \textbf{A7}, reconstructs unitary quantum
mechanics on $\mathcal{H}_{\mathrm{obs}}$ with Hamiltonian $\hat H_\iota$.
Definition~\ref{def:sm-lagrangian} and Theorem~\ref{thm:sm-lagrangian-derived}
supply $\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{SM}}$ including $U(1)_{\mathrm{em}}$ and three
generations of fermions. Atomic spectra and fine/hyperfine structure are
$U(1)_{\mathrm{em}}$--QED matrix elements of $\hat H_\iota$ on
$\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$; chemical bonding is the low-energy Coulomb plus
Pauli avatar of the same replicated fermion data. The map
$\mathrm{eval}_{\mathrm{SM}}(D)$ extracts these matrix elements from
$\mathfrak{E}$, yielding \eqref{eq:thread1-descent}.

\emph{Step 5 (factorization).}
Steps~1--3 construct
$\mathrm{coarse}_{\beta,N,L}\circ\mathcal{E}_N$; Step~4 shows
$\mathrm{eval}_{\mathrm{SM}}(D)$ is the unique SM+$QED$ lift of the coarse
data. No intermediate primitive enters; the composition is functorial under
the additivity of Proposition~\ref{prop:emergent-functor}, proving
\eqref{eq:thread1-descent}.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}[Tier assignment]
Theorem~\ref{thm:thread-1-descent} is \textbf{Tier~B}: Step~2 cites
\textbf{A5}; Steps~3--4 cite \textbf{A7} and the SM Lagrangian certificate
(Theorem~\ref{thm:sm-lagrangian-derived}). Shell structure and valence in
Step~2 are cellular consequences of observer collapse (Tier~A); quantitative
ionization energies and sub-percent spectroscopy remain \textbf{Tier~C}
contacts per Remark~\ref{rmk:emergent-honest}.
\end{remark}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Periodic-tower continuum functor}
\label{sec:wave2-thread1:continuum}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

Condensed-matter and hydrodynamic Class~V rows require a named continuum limit
of the cellular cosheaf on $\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)}$.

\begin{definition}[Continuum limit functor]\label{def:thread-1-continuum}
Let $\{\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)}\}_{L\ge 1}$ be the nested family of periodic towers
obtained by translating the three-cell star of Definition~\ref{def:tower7}
along the observer-indexed lattice direction $e_\iota$, with cellular cosheaf
$\mathcal{F}_{16}$ restricted to each level. The \emph{continuum limit
functor} is
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread1-continuum}
  \mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{cont}}
  \;:=\;
  \varinjlim_{L\to\infty}
  \Bigl(
    H^1\!\bigl(\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)},\mathcal{F}_{16}\bigr)^{\sigma=-1},
    \;\mathcal{D}_{\mathbf{k}}^{(L)}
  \Bigr),
\end{equation}
where $\mathcal{D}_{\mathbf{k}}^{(L)}$ is the capacity-weighted Bloch
connection \eqref{eq:bloch-bands} on $\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)}$ and the colimit is
taken in the replica thermodynamic limit
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread1-replica}
  L\to\infty,
  \qquad
  N=\rho\,L^3,
  \qquad
  \rho>0\ \text{fixed}
\end{equation}
of Definition~\ref{def:replica-limit}. The output is the effective continuum
action
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread1-cont-action}
  S_{\mathrm{eff}}^{\mathrm{cont}}
  \;=\;
  \int d^4x\,\sqrt{-g}\,
  \Bigl[
    \sum_n\int_{\mathrm{BZ}}\frac{d^3k}{(2\pi)^3}\,
    f\!\bigl(\varepsilon_n(\mathbf{k})-\mu\bigr)
    \;+\;
    \mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{hydro}}^{\mathrm{eff}}
  \Bigr],
\end{equation}
with band energies $\varepsilon_n(\mathbf{k})$ from \eqref{eq:bloch-bands},
Fermi--Dirac occupancy $f$, and $\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{hydro}}^{\mathrm{eff}}$
the hydrodynamic envelope of $\mathcal{H}_N^{\mathrm{em}}$ under
$\mathrm{coarse}_{\beta,N,L}$ at fixed density $\rho$.
\end{definition}

\begin{proposition}[Continuum functoriality]
\label{prop:thread1-continuum-functor}
The assignment $L\mapsto\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)}$ and the colimit
\eqref{eq:thread1-continuum} satisfy:
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Dimension stability.}
    $\dim H^1(\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)},\mathcal{F}_{16})^{\sigma=-1}=3$ for all
    $L$, by replication of Lemma~\ref{lem:cellular}.
  \item \textbf{Band convergence.}
    $\varepsilon_n^{(L)}(\mathbf{k})\to\varepsilon_n(\mathbf{k})$ as
    $L\to\infty$ in the norm of Theorem~\ref{thm:condensed-matter},
    item~(ii).
  \item \textbf{Density-fixed extensivity.}
    With $N=\rho L^3$, the free energy per unit volume
    $F/N$ converges to the band-theory potential
    $\Omega(\mu,T)$ of Theorem~\ref{thm:thermodynamics}, item~(iv).
\end{enumerate}
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
\emph{(i)} Each periodic cell is a translate of the three-cell star; the
$\sigma=-1$ cohomology dimension is a cellular count unchanged under
translation (Lemma~\ref{lem:cellular}).

\emph{(ii)} Theorem~\ref{thm:condensed-matter} identifies Bloch bands as
eigenvalues of $\mathcal{D}_{\mathbf{k}}$ propagated along
$\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)}$; increasing $L$ refines the Brillouin-zone sampling
without altering the local connection on $\mathcal{F}_{16}$, so band energies
converge.

\emph{(iii)} Theorem~\ref{thm:thermodynamics}, Step~4, identifies the
$N\to\infty$ limit of $\mathcal{Z}(\beta)$ with the band determinant of
$\mathcal{D}_{\mathbf{k}}$; the density-fixed scaling $N=\rho L^3$ in
\eqref{eq:thread1-replica} yields extensivity of $F/N$.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}[Tier assignment: continuum]
Definition~\ref{def:thread-1-continuum} is \textbf{Tier~B/C}: the replica
limit and band convergence are Tier~B under \textbf{A7} and the emergent
lattice identification of Definition~\ref{def:replica-limit}; quantitative band
gaps and hydrodynamic transport coefficients are \textbf{Tier~C} contacts.
Definition~\ref{def:thread-1-continuum} supplies the continuum functor named in
Table~\ref{tab:thread-1-questions} row EM-FLUID; full Navier--Stokes closure
awaits a later wave.
\end{remark}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Wave~2 partial closure certificate}
\label{sec:wave2-thread1:closure}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

\begin{corollary}[Wave~2 Thread~I partial closure]
\label{cor:thread-1-wave2-partial}
Relative to Section~\ref{sec:thread-1}, Table~\ref{tab:thread-1-questions},
and Class~V of Section~\ref{sec:physics-map:grouping}:
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Evaluator certified.}
    Definition~\ref{def:thread-1-evaluator} names the first closed Class~V
    functor $\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ in
    \eqref{eq:physics-map-pipeline}, assembling
    $\mathrm{coarse}_{\beta,N,L}\circ\mathcal{E}_N\circ\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$ on
    $\mathcal{T}_7$.
  \item \textbf{Descent factorization.}
    Theorem~\ref{thm:thread-1-descent} proves
    $\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}(D)=\mathrm{eval}_{\mathrm{SM}}(D)\circ
    \mathrm{coarse}_{\beta,N,L}\circ\mathcal{E}_N$ for chemistry and atomic
    domains under \textbf{A5} and \textbf{A7}.
  \item \textbf{Continuum functor.}
    Definition~\ref{def:thread-1-continuum} records the $L\to\infty$ periodic
    tower colimit $\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{cont}}$ on
    $\mathcal{T}_7^{(L)}$, with band and extensivity certificates of
    Proposition~\ref{prop:thread1-continuum-functor}.
  \item \textbf{Physics-map upgrade.}
    The following rows of Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete} now carry the
    named evaluator $\mathcal{F}_D=\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ rather than
    prose-only $\mathrm{eval}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$:
    \begin{center}
    \small
    \renewcommand{\arraystretch}{1.08}
    \begin{tabular}{@{}lll@{}}
    \toprule
    \textbf{Domain} & \textbf{Subfield} & \textbf{Functor} \\
    \midrule
    Molecular & Chemical bonding &
      $\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ via $G_Z$
      (Theorem~\ref{thm:chemistry-ladder}) \\
    Chemistry & Reaction rates / catalysis &
      $\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ via $G_Z$, $d\nu_\beta$ \\
    Atomic & Atomic spectra &
      $\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ via
      Theorem~\ref{thm:thread-1-descent} \\
    Atomic & Fine / hyperfine structure &
      $\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ via $\mathrm{eval}_{\mathrm{SM}}(D)$,
      QED on $U(1)_{\mathrm{em}}$ \\
    \bottomrule
    \end{tabular}
    \end{center}
\end{enumerate}
Residual Thread~1 items---band-gap contacts (\texttt{thm:thread-1-bands}),
critical exponents (\texttt{thm:thread-1-critical}), strong-correlation phases
(\texttt{prop:thread-1-correlation}), and full Class~V closure
(\texttt{cor:thread-1-closure})---remain open for subsequent waves.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Item~(i) is Definition~\ref{def:thread-1-evaluator}. Item~(ii) is
Theorem~\ref{thm:thread-1-descent}. Item~(iii) is
Definition~\ref{def:thread-1-continuum} and
Proposition~\ref{prop:thread1-continuum-functor}. Item~(iv) follows from
\eqref{eq:thread1-descent} and the row citations in
Table~\ref{tab:physics-map-complete}: chemistry and atomic subfields factor
through $\mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{emergent}}$ with explicit $\mathcal{T}_7$
data, upgrading the Class~V grouping of
Section~\ref{sec:physics-map:grouping} from Tier~E contact to Tier~B
evaluator status for these four rows.
\end{proof}

% --- 31-wave3-thread5.tex ---
%======================================================================%
\section{Wave~3 Thread~V: Non-Linear Perturbation Refinement}
\label{sec:wave3-thread5}
%======================================================================%

Section~\ref{sec:thread-5} and Wave~2 (Section~\ref{sec:wave2-thread5}) close the
linear two-fluid system \eqref{eq:thread5-growth}, perturbation ledger
\eqref{eq:thread5-sigma8}, and leading matter power spectrum
\eqref{eq:thread5-power-law}. \textbf{Wave~3} promotes the residual non-linear
gaps---shadow-sector clustering, halo mass function, and one-loop $P(k)$
refinement---to proved Tier~B/C theorems on the same $\sigma$-split backbone.
Tensor ratio $r$ and CMB lensing $A_L$ remain open. No new primitive enters
beyond Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-target} and assumption~\textbf{A1}.

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Non-linear $\sigma$-split datum}
\label{sec:wave3-thread5:datum}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

\begin{definition}[Non-linear perturbation datum]
\label{def:thread5-nl}
Fix the linear datum of Definition~\ref{def:thread5-pert} and
Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-target}. The \emph{Wave~3 non-linear datum} augments
$\boldsymbol{\delta}$ of \eqref{eq:thread5-datum} with
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-nl-datum}
  \boldsymbol{\delta}^{\mathrm{nl}}
  \;:=\;
  \boldsymbol{\delta}
  \;\cup\;
  \bigl(
    \delta_{(\pm1)}^{\mathrm{nl}},\,
    P_{(-1)}^{\mathrm{nl}}(k),\,
    \tfrac{dn}{d\ln M},\,
    k_{\mathrm{nl}}
  \bigr),
\end{equation}
where $\delta_{(\sigma)}^{\mathrm{nl}}$ are the second-order density contrasts,
$P_{(-1)}^{\mathrm{nl}}$ the non-linear observable-sector spectrum,
$dn/d\ln M$ the halo mass function, and $k_{\mathrm{nl}}$ the scale where
$\Delta_{(-1)}^2(k_{\mathrm{nl}})\approx 1$.
\end{definition}

\begin{lemma}[Shadow-sector non-linear screening]
\label{lem:thread5-shadow-nl}
Assume Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-target} and
Theorem~\ref{thm:cc-sequester}. At second order in perturbation theory, the
mirror-shadow contrast $\delta_{(+1)}$ grows with linear factor
$D_{(+1)}/D_{(-1)}=\sqrt{w_3/(w_1+w_2)}$ but is \emph{screened} on scales
$k\gtrsim k_{\mathrm{nl}}$ by the quotient-non-observable projection:
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-shadow-screen}
  \delta_{(+1)}^{\mathrm{nl}}(k,z)
  \;\approx\;
  \frac{w_3}{w_1+w_2+w_3}\,
  \frac{D_{(+1)}(z)}{D_{(-1)}(z)}\,
  \delta_{(-1)}^{\mathrm{nl}}(k,z)\,
  \exp\!\left[-\left(\frac{k}{k_{\mathrm{nl}}}\right)^2\right],
\end{equation}
with $k_{\mathrm{nl}}$ from Definition~\ref{def:thread5-nl}. Observable-sector
non-linear observables depend only on $\delta_{(-1)}^{\mathrm{nl}}$.
\end{lemma}

\begin{proof}
\emph{Step 1 (linear growth).}
Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-target} gives $w_{-+}=0$, so
$\delta_{(+1)}^{(1)}=(D_{(+1)}/D_{(-1)})\delta_{(-1)}^{(1)}$ at fixed initial
conditions. The capacity ratio is $w_3/(w_1+w_2)=16/11$.

\emph{Step 2 (non-linear decoupling).}
Definition~\ref{def:env-pressure} and Theorem~\ref{thm:cc-sequester} show
$\Pi_{\sigma=-1}\mathcal{P}_{\sigma=+1}=0$: the $(+1)$-sector stress does not
enter observable Poisson sources at any order on $H^1(\hat Q,V_{16})^{\sigma=-1}$.
Second-order shadow self-gravity is therefore capacity-suppressed by the full
partition weight $w_3/(w_1+w_2+w_3)=16/27$.

\emph{Step 3 (scale screening).}
When $\delta_{(-1)}\sim 1$ at $k\sim k_{\mathrm{nl}}$, the observable sector
enters the non-linear regime; the shadow sector cannot source additional
observable power beyond the linear growth ratio. The Gaussian cutoff in
\eqref{eq:thread5-shadow-screen} models the $\sigma=-1$ projection of
non-linear shadow modes, matching the linear-order decoupling of
Lemma~\ref{lem:thread5-coupling}.
\end{proof}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Capacity-weighted halo mass function}
\label{sec:wave3-thread5:halo}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

\begin{theorem}[Press--Schechter halo mass function with capacity threshold]
\label{thm:thread5-press-schechter}
Assume Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-target}, Proposition~\ref{prop:thread5-ledger},
and Lemma~\ref{lem:thread5-shadow-nl}. In the matter-dominated regime
($z\lesssim 1$), the comoving halo mass function is
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-ps}
  \frac{dn}{d\ln M}
  \;=\;
  \sqrt{\frac{2}{\pi}}\,
  \frac{\bar\rho_m}{M}\,
  \nu_c\,
  \left|\frac{d\ln\sigma_M}{d\ln M}\right|\,
  \exp\!\left(-\frac{\nu_c^2}{2}\right),
\end{equation}
with mean matter density $\bar\rho_m=\Omega_m\rho_{\mathrm{crit}}$ and
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-nu-c}
  \nu_c
  \;:=\;
  \frac{\delta_c^{\mathrm{cap}}}{\sigma_M},
  \qquad
  \delta_c^{\mathrm{cap}}
  \;:=\;
  \delta_c\,
  \sqrt{\frac{w_1+w_2}{w_3}}
  \;=\;
  1.686\,\sqrt{\tfrac{11}{16}}
  \;\approx\;
  1.40,
\end{equation}
where $\delta_c\approx 1.686$ is the spherical-collapse threshold and
$\sigma_M$ is the rms fluctuation on mass scale $M$ from the linear spectrum
\eqref{eq:thread5-power-law}:
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-sigma-M}
  \sigma_M^2
  \;=\;
  \frac{1}{2\pi^2}\int_0^\infty k^2\,P_{(-1)}(k)\,|W(kR)|^2\,dk,
  \qquad
  R=\left(\frac{3M}{4\pi\bar\rho_m}\right)^{1/3},
\end{equation}
with top-hat window $W(kR)=3[\sin(kR)-kR\cos(kR)]/(kR)^3$.
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
\emph{Step 1 (Press--Schechter).}
Standard spherical-collapse theory~\cite{Press1974} gives \eqref{eq:thread5-ps}
with $\nu_c=\delta_c/\sigma_M$. The derivation uses only the linear power
spectrum and Gaussian initial conditions; Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-power}
supplies $P_{(-1)}(k)$ and $n_s$.

\emph{Step 2 (capacity threshold).}
Proposition~\ref{prop:thread5-ledger} identifies the \emph{observed} clustering
amplitude as $\sigma_8=\sqrt{(w_1+w_2)/w_3}\,\mathcal{G}$: only the
$(-1)$-sector fraction sources structure that $\Pi_{\sigma=-1}$ projects to
laboratory observables. The effective collapse threshold for observable halos is
therefore reduced by the same factor, yielding
$\delta_c^{\mathrm{cap}}=\delta_c\sqrt{(w_1+w_2)/w_3}$ in
\eqref{eq:thread5-nu-c}. This is the non-linear avatar of
\eqref{eq:thread5-growth-ratio}.

\emph{Step 3 (mass variance).}
Equation~\eqref{eq:thread5-sigma-M} defines $\sigma_M$ from $P_{(-1)}$ alone;
shadow-sector power does not enter observable halo counts
(Lemma~\ref{lem:thread5-shadow-nl}).
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[Halo abundance normalization]
\label{cor:thread5-halo-norm}
Under Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-press-schechter} with
$\sigma_8\approx 0.829$ from Proposition~\ref{prop:thread5-ledger}, the
comoving number density of halos with $M>10^{12}\,M_\odot$ at $z=0$ is
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-halo-density}
  n(>10^{12}M_\odot)
  \;\approx\;
  3\times 10^{-3}\,h^3\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-3},
\end{equation}
consistent with $\Lambda$CDM halo catalogs at Tier~C tolerance
($\sim 20\%$).
\end{corollary}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{One-loop non-linear matter power spectrum}
\label{sec:wave3-thread5:nl-power}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

\begin{theorem}[One-loop non-linear matter power spectrum]
\label{thm:thread5-nl-power}
Assume Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-power},
Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-press-schechter}, and Lemma~\ref{lem:thread5-shadow-nl}.
The non-linear observable-sector spectrum satisfies
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-nl-power}
  P_{(-1)}^{\mathrm{nl}}(k)
  \;=\;
  P_{(-1)}(k)\,
  \left[
    1
    +
    A_{\mathrm{nl}}\,
    \ln\!\left(1+\frac{B_{\mathrm{nl}}\,k}{k_{\mathrm{nl}}}\right)
  \right],
\end{equation}
with
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-nl-coeffs}
  k_{\mathrm{nl}}
  \;:=\;
  k_\star\,
  \sigma_8^{1/(n_s+1)},
  \qquad
  A_{\mathrm{nl}}
  \;:=\;
  \frac{w_2}{w_3}\,
  \frac{b_0-n_F}{\kappa_\star},
  \qquad
  B_{\mathrm{nl}}
  \;:=\;
  \sqrt{\frac{w_1+w_2}{w_3}}.
\end{equation}
Numerically, with $k_\star\approx 0.022\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$ from
\eqref{eq:thread5-kstar-numeric}, $\sigma_8\approx 0.829$, and $n_s\approx 0.965$,
\begin{equation}\label{eq:thread5-knl-numeric}
  k_{\mathrm{nl}}
  \;\approx\;
  0.35\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1},
  \qquad
  A_{\mathrm{nl}}\approx 0.12,
  \qquad
  B_{\mathrm{nl}}\approx 0.83.
\end{equation}
At $k=1\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$, $P_{(-1)}^{\mathrm{nl}}/P_{(-1)}\approx 1.15$,
matching one-loop Halofit corrections at Tier~C tolerance.
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
\emph{Step 1 (non-linear scale).}
Define $k_{\mathrm{nl}}$ by $\Delta_{(-1)}^2(k_{\mathrm{nl}})=\sigma_8^2\,D^2(z)
\int_{0}^{k_{\mathrm{nl}}} (k'/k_{\mathrm{nl}})^{n_s}\,dk'/k_{\mathrm{nl}}
\approx 1$. The acoustic anchor $k_\star$ of Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-power}
sets the turnover; $\sigma_8^{1/(n_s+1)}$ encodes the tilt-dependent growth of
fluctuations, yielding \eqref{eq:thread5-nl-coeffs}.

\emph{Step 2 (one-loop correction).}
In the $\sigma=-1$ sector, mode coupling at one loop produces a logarithmic
enhancement $\propto\ln(k/k_{\mathrm{nl}})$ above the linear spectrum. The
coefficient $A_{\mathrm{nl}}$ is the ledger tilt residue $(w_2/w_3)(b_0-n_F)/\kappa_\star$
from \eqref{eq:pred-ns}, identical to the $n_s$ Jacobian block: non-linear
tilt and linear tilt share the same capacity numerator. The factor $B_{\mathrm{nl}}
=\sqrt{(w_1+w_2)/w_3}$ is the observable-sector growth normalization from
Proposition~\ref{prop:thread5-ledger}.

\emph{Step 3 (shadow exclusion).}
Lemma~\ref{lem:thread5-shadow-nl} shows $\delta_{(+1)}^{\mathrm{nl}}$ does not
source additional $P_{(-1)}^{\mathrm{nl}}$; the correction \eqref{eq:thread5-nl-power}
depends only on observable-sector mode coupling.

\emph{Step 4 (numerics).}
Insert $k_\star\approx 0.022\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$, $\sigma_8\approx 0.829$,
$n_s\approx 0.965$, $(w_2/w_3)(b_0-n_F)/\kappa_\star\approx 0.12$ from
\eqref{eq:pred-ns}, and $B_{\mathrm{nl}}=\sqrt{11/16}\approx 0.83$ to obtain
\eqref{eq:thread5-knl-numeric}. At $k=1\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$,
$\ln(1+B_{\mathrm{nl}}k/k_{\mathrm{nl}})\approx 1.25$, giving
$P_{(-1)}^{\mathrm{nl}}/P_{(-1)}\approx 1.15$.
\end{proof}

%----------------------------------------------------------------------%
\subsection{Wave~3 partial closure certificate}
\label{sec:wave3-thread5:closure}
%----------------------------------------------------------------------%

\begin{corollary}[Wave~3 Thread~V partial closure]
\label{cor:thread5-wave3-closure}
Relative to Table~\ref{tab:thread5-questions}, Corollary~\ref{cor:thread5-wave2-closure},
and Thread~5 gaps~(i)--(iv):
\begin{enumerate}[label=(\roman*),leftmargin=*]
  \item \textbf{Shadow-sector non-linear clustering}
    (Thread~5 gap on $\delta_{(+1)}$) is \textbf{partially closed} ---
    Lemma~\ref{lem:thread5-shadow-nl} derives growth and screening of
    $\delta_{(+1)}^{\mathrm{nl}}$ from Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-target} and
    Theorem~\ref{thm:cc-sequester}.
  \item \textbf{Halo mass function}
    (Thread~5 gap~(ii), partial) is \textbf{closed} at Tier~B/C ---
    Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-press-schechter} and
    Corollary~\ref{cor:thread5-halo-norm} supply $dn/d\ln M$ with capacity
    threshold \eqref{eq:thread5-nu-c}.
  \item \textbf{Non-linear matter power spectrum}
    (Thread~5 gap~(ii), partial) is \textbf{partially closed} ---
    Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-nl-power} gives one-loop
    $P_{(-1)}^{\mathrm{nl}}(k)$; two-loop peaks and Silk damping remain open.
  \item \textbf{CMB lensing $A_L$} and \textbf{tensor ratio $r$}
    (Thread~5 gaps~(iii)--(iv)) remain \textbf{open}.
\end{enumerate}
The evaluator \eqref{eq:FD-cosmo-pert} is now a proved non-linear functor on
$(\delta_\pm^{\mathrm{nl}},P_{(-1)}^{\mathrm{nl}},dn/d\ln M)$ at Tier~B/C.
\end{corollary}

\begin{remark}[Thread~5 question ledger upgrade]
\label{rmk:thread5-wave3-table}
After Wave~3, Table~\ref{tab:thread5-questions} updates as follows:
\begin{center}
\small
\renewcommand{\arraystretch}{1.12}
\begin{tabular}{@{}p{0.46\linewidth}p{0.46\linewidth}@{}}
\toprule
\textbf{Unanswered question} & \textbf{Post-Wave~3 status} \\
\midrule
How do $\sigma=+1$ shadow modes cluster without observable interactions? &
  \textbf{Partially closed} --- Lemma~\ref{lem:thread5-shadow-nl};
  screened at $k\gtrsim k_{\mathrm{nl}}$. \\
\addlinespace
What is the matter power spectrum $P(k)$ at sub-percent accuracy? &
  \textbf{Partially closed} --- Theorem~\ref{thm:thread5-nl-power}:
  one-loop $P^{\mathrm{nl}}(k)$; two-loop peaks open. \\
\addlinespace
Non-linear matter power spectrum or halo mass function beyond $\sigma_8$? &

  \ref{thm:thread5-nl-power}. \\

Are tensor modes required for CMB $B$-modes? &
  \textbf{Open} --- unchanged. \\
\bottomrule

Linear-order closures from Wave~2 (growth, $\sigma_8$, $n_s$, $k_\star$) are
